The World's Largest Merchant Ship, the Queen Mary, Is Launched 27

Clydebank. The world's largest merchant ship, the Queen Mary, slowly sailed out of the shipyard of John Brown & Company this morning at 10:10 am, towed by seven tugboats. After 15 minutes, it entered the river and then sailed along the river by its own power. Four tugboats followed it into the sea and went to Southampton. Many people watched along the river and cheered loudly. (Reuter Telegram on the 24th)

London. The new ship "Queen Mary" of White Star Line, totaling 87,730 tons, is more than 1,200 tons larger than the French Normandy, but this new ship is 1,018 feet long, 56 feet longer than the French ship. Today, this new ship will enter the sea and go to Southampton for its first voyage, so it is expected that many people will go to Clydebank today to watch it sail. At that time, eight tugboats will tow it into the sea, and four will follow it. The new ship is scheduled to go to New York from Southampton on May 27 for its maiden voyage. It is expected that it can prove that it is the fastest merchant ship in the world, with a speed of 30 nautical miles per hour, which is equal to 34.5 miles on land. According to reports, the French ship Normandy traveled from Southampton to New York across the Atlantic Ocean last June in four days, three hours, and five minutes, with an average speed of 29.98 nautical miles. Although the average speed of the Queen Mary's normal navigation is set at 29 nautical miles, it can reach an average speed of 34 nautical miles on its maiden voyage. However, this is not the highest speed of the new ship. The ship has 27 steam boilers and 16 turbines. If all are started, the speed of the ship can be more than 40 nautical miles per hour. The ship will have two captains, who will be jointly responsible. This is a pioneering move in the shipping industry. This ship was designed by the best scientific minds in the UK, and it was built by skilled workers. 300,000 people, directly and indirectly, worked on this ship. (Reuter Telegram on the 24th)

The Shijingshan Power Plant's waterway was destroyed by the ice mountain, and the electric light company has added 500 workers to chisel ice. (Special Telegram on the 24th)

Rural Life Miscellany, Chief Editor: Yu Qingtang, The Burden of Land Tax on Farmers in the Southeast of Wuxi (Part 2), Weng Zushan, Four: An Unfinished Story 38

"The nature of Chinese farmers is docile," I didn't say that wrong. However, we cannot deny that "you can't squeeze oil from sugar cane dregs." When the amount demanded by unscrupulous tax collectors exceeds their—the farmers'—ability to bear it, even the most "docile" farmers will rise up and fight like cornered beasts!

Here, let us unfold an unfinished tragic story:

One cold, windy, and bleak night, driven by my duties, I went to a public school about four li away from my residence to see them attending night classes. After class, many familiar but not entirely known farmers surrounded me to talk. Among this sincere group, I noticed a middle-aged farmer named Junquan, which made me think of his wife—Yu Que's—who was currently detained in the county government facing charges. I had heard about this a month ago, but I had forgotten about it after hearing it at the time. Now that I met him in person, I wanted to ask him for details.

"Ah, Junquan! Has your wife been released?"

"Hmm, no!" was a bitter and heavy reply.

"It's been sixty-two days today!" Someone behind me added resentfully.

"Oh, so do you actually owe land tax?"

"I don't owe! Not only do I not owe, but they used to overcharge me four or five yuan every year. It was even worse the year before last, they overcharged me nine yuan. I haven't even received the second installment of the receipt, and he said that the rice I gave him was not good."

"Since you don't owe and they're still extorting you, why did they arrest your wife?"

"It's everyone who harmed him!" Twenty or thirty voices spoke almost simultaneously.

"How so?"

"Because we have been extorted by the tax collector every year and really can't afford it, some people initiated the idea of going to the granary ourselves to pay this year. Who knew the news would leak out, and he—referring to the tax collector—took action first!"

A young farmer explained to me enthusiastically. Everyone's facial expressions were very tense.

"Also, this year the tax collector withheld the receipt. I went to the county myself to pay. The granary said that I couldn't pay without the receipt. Later, I hardened my heart and argued with them. I said, 'If you don't let me pay, I'll go to the provincial government to sue!' They had no choice but to call an old gentleman to persuade me and help me check the amount of land tax, and as a result, I paid eleven yuan and twenty cents. Therefore, the tax collector hated me even more!" This was Junquan's words.

"Was there a court hearing?"

"No! The petition to request a court hearing has been submitted five times!"

"Five petitions have gone to the City God Temple!"

Everyone smiled unnaturally and was immediately surrounded by a solemn atmosphere again.

I was astonished! The county government detained a farm woman for more than sixty days for no reason, without questioning or releasing her. What kind of logic is this?

After the solar new year, I ran into a farmer from the aforementioned village alley on the road. According to him, Junquan's wife was detained for sixty-six days before he was summoned for questioning, and the questions were completely irrelevant. At this time, his wife was sick, and Junquan went to replace her. Now it has been more than twenty days! I don't know when this lawsuit will end and when he will be released from prison?

Tonight is the twenty-sixth day of the lunar December (the couple has been detained for a total of ninety-four days). The sharp west wind intermittently brings the barking of cold dogs. The clock ticks in the freezing air, which makes me think of Junquan, who is suffering in prison right now. I'm afraid he won't be able to go home for the "New Year's Eve dinner" this year, will he?

Five. Conclusion

The aforementioned various facts are enough to illustrate the ruthlessness of the tax collectors' methods of harassing the people and the miserable situation of those who are exploited and left to be slaughtered. In the past, I have repeatedly seen reports about the exorbitant taxes and levies in provinces such as Sichuan, and at that time, I thought that this was only a unique phenomenon under the situation of warlord separatism. Now I know that "crows are black all over the world."

Italy, Austria, Hungary Sign Tripartite Agreement of a Political, Economic and Cultural Nature 39

Rome. Italy, Austria, and Hungary signed a tripartite agreement today to extend the validity of the 1934 tripartite agreement, consolidate the political and economic relations of the three countries, and assist each other publicly, similar in nature, but with more ambiguous wording. (23rd, Guomin Electric)

Rome. It is now believed that one of the clauses of the agreement signed by Italy, Austria, and Hungary today is that if the League of Nations implements sanctions against Germany, the three countries will not participate. It is heard that the statement also declares the determination to maintain Austria's independence and invites other countries to join the agreement, apparently intending to make Austria and Czechoslovakia cooperate more closely. The three countries also agree to increase commercial relations with each other in economic terms. The agreement will be announced today. (24th, Reuters)

Rome. It was officially announced that Prime Minister Mussolini met with Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Hungarian Prime Minister Gömbös at the Palazzo Venezia this afternoon to sign a protocol as an annex to the tripartite agreement of March 17, 1934 between Italy, Austria, and Hungary. The full text will be announced tomorrow afternoon. The final communiqué on the course of the talks stated that "the authorities of the three countries are sincere and can understand each other." As far as the general public knows, the authorities of Italy, Austria, and Hungary have already agreed to adopt a common stance on foreign policy and have agreed that the Danube countries may join the 1934 tripartite agreement under certain conditions, but Italy is unwilling to establish an agreement with countries participating in sanctions while the sanction measures continue to be implemented. In the future, any agreement shall recognize the principle of equal rights and be concluded within the scope of the League of Nations. (23rd, Havas)

Rome. After the authorities of Italy, Austria, and Hungary signed the protocol yesterday, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini met with Austrian Chancellor Schuschnigg and Foreign Minister Guido Schmidt for an hour at 12:00 noon today. It is expected that a communiqué will still be issued this afternoon with some explanations. According to sources in political circles, although the authorities of the three countries have decided that the countries in the Danube River basin may join the 1934 tripartite agreement under certain conditions, the protocol signed yesterday was only signed by Italy, Austria, and Hungary. According to well-informed sources, during the talks, the authorities of the three countries also occasionally mentioned the issue of rearming Austria and Hungary. Most members of the Austrian and Hungarian delegations are scheduled to return to their countries this evening, but the two prime ministers, Schuschnigg and Gömbös, plan to stay here for a few days in a private capacity. Pope Pius XI is scheduled to receive Gömbös this evening. (24th, Havas)

Rome. After signing the protocol yesterday, the authorities of Italy, Austria, and Hungary signed another protocol today, stipulating that a standing conference be organized by the foreign ministers of the countries concerned to meet periodically. This conference is actually similar to the standing political conference of the Little Entente countries. (24th, Havas News Agency)

Germany Rejects Proposal, British and French Opinions Differ Again, French Foreign Minister Notifies Britain of No Further Concessions, League of Nations Administrative Council Meeting Extended Again 40

Berlin. The German representative to the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting, Ribbentrop, flew to London at 2:08 PM today with the government's reply to the Locarno Four-Power Pact. No one knows what the content of this reply is. Political figures are unwilling to comment on it. However, semi-official sources claim that in addition to carrying a written reply, Ribbentrop intends to provide supplementary oral explanations at the Administrative Council meeting. Foreign affairs figures believe that Germany will reject several measures of the Locarno Four-Power Pact and adopt delaying tactics on several other measures. In short, the German government's reply will only be released after Ribbentrop delivers it to British Foreign Secretary Eden for review. (24th, Havas)

London. France formally notified Britain today, stating that it does not want to make any concessions to the Four-Power Pact and is unwilling to discuss any counter-proposals from Germany in London. This proves that differences have arisen in the positions of Britain and France, making it hopeless to resolve the situation caused by Germany's actions for a while. It is heard that General Ribbentrop, the German representative, will stay in London for several days after returning to London. If there is hope for a compromise after the negotiations, the Locarno powers will continue to meet in Lausanne. The League of Nations is becoming increasingly impatient because the Locarno powers have been unable to reach a compromise with Germany. The Administrative Council meeting this afternoon may decide to announce the postponement of the Administrative Council meeting and reconvene as usual in May. (24th, Reuters)

London. The League of Nations Administrative Council was originally scheduled to discuss the Locarno Four-Power Pact at 4:00 PM today. Because the German representative, Ribbentrop, did not arrive from Berlin until 2:00 PM today, it may not be in time. Therefore, the Administrative Council has decided to postpone the meeting. However, the general public believes that the real reason for the postponement of the Administrative Council meeting is that the opinions of the countries concerned differ, causing many difficulties. (24th, Havas)

France's Attitude is Firm, Britain and Germany are Shocked, Italy Hopes to Profit from It 41

Paris. Regarding the Locarno Four-Power Pact, rumors that the government has decided not to discuss any counter-proposals that Germany may put forward have been confirmed by responsible persons, who said that Premier Sarraut and Foreign Minister Flandin have repeatedly stated that France does not want to conduct negotiations under threat and that the international rule of law must be restored. As for the proposal in the German memorandum to submit various suggestions for discussion, France is not determined to reject it, but requires that it be done in an international conference. This is what Foreign Minister Flandin and Minister Without Portfolio Peng Gu agreed with the representatives of Britain, Belgium, and Italy at the Locarno conference in London a few days ago. Although the conditions stipulated in the Locarno Four-Power Pact have been approved by the British Cabinet, they must still be implemented. (24th, Havas)

London. News from Paris today said that the French government's will is that France will not make any concessions whatsoever to the agreement reached by the Locarno powers, Britain, France, and Italy, in London. Germany must accept it or reject it. The London delegations were greatly shocked by this news. It is also heard that French Foreign Minister Flandin said that he does not want to return to London to discuss Germany's answer. The London delegations now feel that this attitude will endanger the overall situation and make a compromise with Germany practically impossible. Officials have not announced this news, but it has been said that Flandin and Belgian Prime Minister Zeeland will not return to London. Any negotiations on Germany's answer will be conducted through ordinary diplomatic channels. (24th, Reuters)

Berlin. News that French Foreign Minister Flandin refused to consider any answers that Germany put forward to the Four-Power Memorandum caused a shock in political circles here, and it was seen that Flandin's attitude contradicted the remarks made by British Foreign Secretary Eden in the Lower House yesterday. When the British Foreign Secretary mentioned the Four-Power Memorandum in the House, he said that if the German government believed that it could not accept the conditions of the four powers and put forward an answer, the British government would welcome it. (24th, Reuters)

Paris. France is preparing today to deal with German Head of State Hitler's rejection of the Locarno powers' proposal. Premier Sarraut, Foreign Minister Flandin, and other cabinet members discussed the actions to be taken in the future today. Official sources said that if Britain, Belgium, and Italy do not want to support France's position, France will unilaterally implement economic sanctions against Germany to prevent Germany from obtaining the necessary foreign funds. (23rd, Guomin Electric)

London. When the Lower House met today, Prime Minister Baldwin replied to a question about the European situation, saying that the British government's main goal is to maintain the principle of respecting the treaty. Foreign Secretary Eden replied to another question, saying that when he spoke with German Representative General Ribbentrop, he clearly stated that the content of the official document he sent to Mr. Ribbentrop was of a suggestive nature. He also said, "I have explained that the British government hopes that the German government can accept it. The British government feels that in any event, the German government should assist the British government in its work to improve the situation by making constructive contributions." The British Ambassador stationed in Berlin has been instructed to explain to the German Foreign Minister in the same language. The German government's reply has not yet arrived. (23rd, Reuters)

London. Lord Privy Seal Halifax, one of the British representatives who participated in the four-country discussions in Paris and London, said in a speech in Bristol yesterday that we do not want to surround Germany, nor do we want to establish secret treaties, but we want European cooperation that Germany can freely join. The proposal made to Germany by the signatories of the Locarno Pact is not an ultimatum that Germany must accept, but if the German government believes that it cannot accept it in any way, the signatories can of course ask the German government to put forward other equally effective methods to show Germany's true contribution to the resolution of this matter. As far as the British government is concerned, any answer from Germany can be given the most careful consideration. The only wish of the British government and people is to exert all its power to maintain peace in Europe and to create peace based on respect for treaties and mutual understanding. This is the essence of British foreign policy. Speaking of the German reasons stated by German Representative Ribbentrop at the League of Nations Administrative Council meeting, Mr. Hall said that the German representative's remarks have many aspects that can arouse sympathy, but no matter what sympathy the British have for what he said, the British concept of respecting the law cannot but condemn the act of directly violating the law. He understands and sympathizes with the anxiety and indignation of France and Belgium caused by the German troops entering the Rhineland. If the first crisis can be mitigated, it is due to the patience of France and Belgium and British Foreign Secretary Eden's unremitting efforts to seek good understanding between the two sides. (24th, Reuters)

Paris. British Foreign Secretary Eden made a statement in the House of Commons this afternoon, in which he said, "When I spoke with German Representative to the League of Nations Administrative Council Ribbentrop, I told him that the draft agreement of the Locarno Conference was of a suggestive nature." Responsible persons in the Ministry of Foreign Affairs here were concerned that Eden's remarks might lead to misunderstandings and that the draft agreement could be reconsidered by the Locarno signatories. They recently stated that the French government has no intention of reconsidering the draft agreement, because Foreign Minister Flandin had previously stated in the House of Representatives that this case is an entire acceptance or rejection, and the entire case should be accepted or rejected. Therefore, Flandin has no need to go to London before Germany provides a clear reply (referring to acceptance or rejection). Even if Germany puts forward a counter-proposal at this time, he will never go to London to negotiate with Germany. Flandin is currently feeling tired due to his hard work in the past few days, so he is scheduled to go to the countryside tomorrow for a short rest. As far as this agency's diplomatic reporter knows, Belgian Prime Minister Zeeland has also adopted the same attitude as Flandin, that is, if Germany puts forward a counter-proposal, Prime Minister Zeeland will never return to London to discuss it. (23rd, Havas)

London. The Administrative Council was originally scheduled to discuss the Locarno Four-Power Pact this afternoon. Because German Representative Ribbentrop may not arrive in time, the meeting may be postponed. According to this agency's special correspondent, the Italian government's delay in approving this agreement is also one of the reasons for the postponement of the Administrative Council meeting. It is generally believed that Italian Prime Minister Mussolini wants to use this opportunity as a bargaining chip. The country has clearly demanded the withdrawal of sanctions as an exchange condition for restoring the Stresa Front of Britain, France, and Italy. Observers claim that Italy has never automatically participated in measures to take coercive measures against Germany and send international troops to occupy the Rhineland region, because Germany did not comply with the League of Nations' sanctions against Italy last year, so Italy wants to use this opportunity to repay it. (24th, Havas)

European Situation Tense, French Funds Escape, German Trade Declines 43

London. Foreign exchange is currently affected by political instability, but the US dollar is particularly strong. The franc is the most vulnerable to attacks in comparison, due to the continued flight of French funds. The British Exchange Equalization Fund is absorbing francs at any time, which is why the pound is weaker than the US dollar. It is said that most of France's liquid funds have been transferred to the United States to seek safety, so the amount of funds escaping from France at present may not be much. However, at least part of the funds newly raised by the French Ministry of Finance will go abroad. The franc's forward discount decreased slightly today to 2.19, but the difference between the forward and spot discounts is still large, because the annual interest rate of selling spot and buying forward is 11.5%. The franc's three-month interest rate rebounded slightly today, due to the settlement of the short side, but not because France will still adhere to the gold standard and improve. (24th, Reuters)

Berlin. The election of the House of Representatives is scheduled for March 29. The government has scheduled large-scale prestige movements for the 27th and 28th. March 28, Saturday, is "National Honor, Freedom, and Peace Day." At 6:30 PM on the same day, Head of State Hitler will deliver his final election speech. Education Broadcasting Special Issue

Youth and Society (Part 2) 82

Professor Sun Benwen, Faculty of Arts, Central University

2. The Responsibility of Youth to Society: Since the position of youth in society is so important, the responsibilities they bear are also very significant. Simply put, the responsibilities of youth to society can be divided into two major aspects: namely, the responsibility to promote the past of society and the responsibility to build the future of society.

First, the responsibility to promote the past of society: Chinese society has left behind many legacies in the past that are worthy of our praise. Three examples can be cited:

China has a long history. The length of Chinese history is unmatched by any other country in modern civilized nations. As we know, there were four cultural centers in the ancient world: namely, Egypt, Babylon, China, and India. And now, only China stands proudly independent in the world. Modern European countries, such as England, France, Germany, and Italy, mostly formed after the Tang and Song dynasties in China. The independence and unification of Germany and Italy are even less than a century old. The independence of the United States is only about one hundred and sixty years old. In China's five thousand years, although dynasties have changed, and disturbances have followed one another, and it has been ravaged by foreign races twice, the cultural history has never been interrupted. This is our

China has a unique culture. There must be indelible fundamental reasons why China can have such a long history. According to our analysis, this fundamental reason lies in China's unique culture. This unique culture has enabled the entire Chinese society to form a spiritually consolidated unity and to adapt automatically to the needs of the times. Therefore, although Chinese society has occasionally experienced periods of prosperity and decline in the past, it has never been fundamentally shaken. At least, this was the case before contact with the West. Simply put, this unique culture has three basic patterns: namely, family-based, self-cultivation-based, and moderation-based.

(A) Family-based culture: The family is the unit of Chinese social organization, including paternal relatives, maternal relatives, and marital relatives, that is, both blood relatives and relatives by marriage. Family relations are the paradigm of interpersonal relationships in Chinese society. All relationships in society are concentrated in the family. Then, the family is extended to society and the nation. Therefore, Mr. Sun Yat-sen said: "Chinese people most worship familism and clanism." He also said: "The Chinese people's solidarity for their families and clans is very strong." The basic spirit that maintains the unity of this family organization is filial piety. All ways of cultivating oneself and governing others are based on filial piety. Therefore, the Classic of Filial Piety says: "Filial piety is the foundation of virtue." It also says: "Filial piety is the law of Heaven, the righteousness of Earth, and the conduct of the people." The Analects also says: "Filial piety and brotherly love are the roots of benevolence." In addition to filial piety, family morality also includes brotherly love, kindness, etc., which is the so-called righteousness of kinship. However, the righteousness of kinship not only extends to the living but also extends to the deceased ancestors, hence the worship of ancestors. As the Doctrine of the Mean says: "Serving the dead as serving the living, serving the departed as serving the existent, is the ultimate filial piety." The Analects also says: "Be cautious in mourning the dead and pursue the memory of the distant ancestors, and the virtue of the people will return to sincerity." Starting from this basic morality of filial piety, it extends beyond the family, and then there is the heart of loyalty and love for the sovereign and the country. The Classic of Filial Piety says: "The gentleman is devoted to filial piety to his parents, so his loyalty can be transferred to the sovereign." It also says: "Serving the sovereign with filial piety is loyalty." The Great Learning says: "Filial piety is the way to serve the sovereign." In short, loyalty is the extension of filial piety. In ancient times, there were monarchs, so loyalty was to the monarch; in modern times, it is loyalty to the country and loyalty to the leader. Further extending to the general society, there is the spirit of regarding all people as siblings and all things as companions. Mencius says: "Love your relatives and be benevolent to the people, be benevolent to the people and love things." He also says: "Treat the young of others as you would your own, and care for the elderly of others as you would your own." The Great Learning says: "Brotherly love is the way to serve elders, and kindness is the way to employ the masses." These are all ways to extend the principle of kinship to society. This process of taking the family as the foundation and extending it to the nation and society is the great way of "managing the family, governing the country, and bringing peace to the world." However, in reality, China has always only reached the level of the family. Beyond the family, it has only become an ideal. Therefore, Mr. Sun Yat-sen said: "The Chinese people's solidarity can only extend to the clan, and has not yet expanded to the nation." To restore the inherent status of the country, we must now, as Mr. Sun said: "Make good use of the inherent groups in China, such as family groups and clan groups, and unite them to form a large national group."

(B) Self-cultivation-based culture: Self-cultivation is the basis of Chinese social ethics and the paradigm of personal cultivation. Family relations are about people-to-people relationships; self-cultivation is about one's relationship with oneself. If everyone in society cultivates themselves, then the family will inevitably be harmonious, and the country will inevitably be well-governed. Therefore, the Great Learning says: "Only when the person is cultivated can the family be regulated; only when the family is regulated can the state be rightly governed." It also says: "From the Son of Heaven down to the common people, all must regard self-cultivation as the root." According to the eight items set in the Great Learning, namely, investigating things, extending knowledge, making the will sincere, rectifying the heart, cultivating oneself, regulating the family, governing the state, and bringing peace to the world. The first five are about one's relationship with oneself, and the last three are about one's relationship with others. Therefore, the self-cultivation-based culture and the family-based culture are originally consistent. However, the self-cultivation-based culture is the foundation of the family-based culture. The steps of self-cultivation are investigating things, extending knowledge, making the will sincere, and rectifying the heart; and the method of self-cultivation is nothing more than overcoming oneself and returning to propriety. Outwardly, one should take rites and righteousness as the norm; inwardly, one should have the effort to overcome oneself. The Book of Rites says: "Rites are what make a person a person." But rites and righteousness must be practiced. Therefore, the Doctrine of the Mean says: "There are three hundred rites and three thousand decorums, which must be practiced by the right person." To practice rites and righteousness, one must overcome oneself. The Analects says: "To overcome oneself and return to propriety is benevolence." It also says: "Do not look at what is contrary to propriety, do not listen to what is contrary to propriety, do not speak what is contrary to propriety, do not move in a way that is contrary to propriety." Because overcoming oneself must start from daily life. The rites of seeing, hearing, speaking, and moving, and the etiquette of sweeping and responding are all efforts to overcome oneself. The key points of overcoming oneself lie in caution when alone and reverence for reality. Because of caution when alone, the Great Learning says: "What ten eyes see and ten hands point at, how awe-inspiring it is!" The Book of Poetry says: "Even in your room, do not be ashamed before the roof." Because of reverence for reality, the Doctrine of the Mean says: "Looking inward and finding no guilt, there is no evil in the will." Mencius says: "To reflect on oneself and be sincere is the greatest joy." In this way, by being cautious when alone and revering reality, one overcomes oneself and returns to propriety, thus achieving the goal of self-cultivation. This is the essence of personal cultivation and the paradigm that everyone in society should follow. It is used to teach children, and teachers use it to teach students, and it has not changed much for thousands of years. In reality, not everyone can fully implement it, but it has become a basic culture in society, which is undoubtedly true. However, since the opening of the sea and contact with Western culture, the standards of self-cultivation in this country have changed.

(C) Moderation-based culture: Moderation is the paradigm for managing affairs and conducting oneself in Chinese society. Family and self-cultivation are about one's relationship with others and oneself; moderation is about one's relationship with things. The meaning of moderation is to be impartial, without excess or deficiency. The Doctrine of the Mean says: "Moderation is the correct way of the world, and constancy is the principle of the world." Moderation is the correct way and principle; therefore, it contains the meaning of rationality. Rationality is not easy, so the Doctrine of the Mean says: "The wise go too far, and the foolish do not go far enough; the virtuous go too far, and the unworthy do not go far enough." It also says: "Moderation is the highest virtue, but few people can maintain it for long." It also says: "The world and the nation can be governed equally; noble rank and wealth can be declined; white blades can be stepped on; but moderation is impossible." But moderation is not only rational but also must be timely. Therefore, the Doctrine of the Mean says: "The gentleman's moderation is that he is timely in his moderation." Timely moderation means being appropriate at all times; it contains the meaning of adapting to the environment. The Analects says: "Speak only when the time is right, and people will not be tired of your words." Mencius says: "Confucius was the sage of timeliness." This "timeliness" means timely moderation, indicating the meaning of adapting to the environment. Since moderation is about adapting to the environment, it has the meaning of evolution. Chinese society was originally evolutionary, and it was the result of the development of moderation culture. Historical books say: "The Three Sovereigns did not follow the music, and the Five Emperors did not follow the rites." Therefore, the Xia dynasty valued loyalty, the Yin dynasty valued simplicity, and the Zhou dynasty valued culture; all were determined according to the needs of adapting to the environment. It can be seen that as times change, society also changes to adapt to them. The Book of Poetry says: "Although Zhou is an old state, its destiny is new." The Great Learning says: "If you can renovate yourself for one day, then do so from day to day, and again from day to day." This means renovating oneself to adapt to the environment; it also contains the meaning of evolution. Moreover, since moderation is neither excessive nor deficient, it has the meaning of harmony. All those who are harmonious must be peaceful. The world recognizes that the Chinese nation is a peaceful nation, which is due to the influence of moderation culture. In short, being able to be harmonious, rational, and adapt to the environment is the way of moderation. The way of moderation is the paradigm for managing affairs and conducting oneself in Chinese society. But in reality, not everyone can follow the way of moderation, but everyone takes it as the standard.

All the three basic cultures mentioned above are unique to China. The family is the paradigm for dealing with people, self-cultivation is the paradigm for dealing with oneself, and moderation is the paradigm for dealing with things. Combining these three paradigms forms a special cultural system, which is the characteristic of Chinese culture. This is the second point we should promote. (To be continued)

Page 9

Miscellaneous Writings on Rural Hubei 83

— Our reporter Cheng Jun

(1) On the Road from Hankou to Puqi

Rural bankruptcy is a widespread phenomenon throughout the country. After the natural and man-made disasters in Hubei, agricultural production has decreased, and farmers have lost their homes. The degree of bankruptcy is actually greater than in other provinces. We live in the city, our ears do not hear the cries of farmers, and our eyes do not see the tragic situation in the countryside. To talk about relief is nothing but self-deception. Therefore, the reporter went to the countryside to investigate the actual situation, so as to know where the crux lies and to explore ways to restore the situation. In addition to agricultural production, farmers' burdens, local disasters, and the sufferings of the masses as the main investigation materials, other water conservancy, dikes, mineral products, education, disaster relief, Qingxiang, Baojia, and other things closely related to the countryside are also within the scope of the investigation.

At six o'clock in the morning on March 20th, I took a boat on the Yuehan Railway from Hankou to cross the river. At that time, the heavy snow had just cleared, the water was calm, and the willow color across the river was vying to send green greetings, which made my dusty heart feel open and bright. At seven o'clock, I got on the train at Xujiapeng in Wuchang. There were so many passengers that it was very crowded. The train carriages were simply equipped and did not pay attention to hygiene. People spit everywhere, and no one interfered. At eight o'clock, the train slowly started. It stopped at Dianyuqiao station and did not start again for more than an hour. At that time, the train carriage was shaking violently, which made people unbearable. I asked and learned that the sleepers on the road were mostly old things from the initial opening of the traffic in the third year of the Republic of China. They were rotten and could not be used, so no wonder. Now that the entire Yuehan Railway is about to open to traffic, this section of the road must be thoroughly rectified. There is a strange phenomenon on the train that is not found on other roads in the country, that is, there are dozens of vendors coming and going like weaving, shouting loudly, like the collapse of Tongshan in the east and the response of the Luoyang bells in the west. When the ticket inspector comes, they all avoid each other, some climbing to the top of the car, as agile as monkeys. When the ticket inspector leaves, they swarm down again, which makes the passengers feel uneasy. These are all poor people who are driven by hunger and cold. Although it is not necessary to strictly ban them, it seems necessary to add some restrictions. There were two passengers in the same car, one in plain clothes and one in military uniform. The military police asked to see their passports. They took out a piece of paper from their arms, which was stamped, and it was from the Wuchang County Government, ordering them to go to Shanpo and other places to collect taxes. I looked at the ticket, and there were dozens of people who were summoned. I smiled and said to the officials that this trip should be able to make a lot of money. They sighed and said that this was a good job in the past few years, but now the villagers have no food to eat, how can they provide a penny? They also said that some of their peers had gone on business trips and were hungry. If what they said is true, then the government is also afraid of the poverty of the people, and the King of Hell is also afraid of the thinness of the ghosts, and the poverty of the countryside can be imagined.

The train arrived at Heshengqiao and had entered Xianning. It is a more prosperous town in the county. Before long, it arrived in Xianning. The city gate is tightly opposite the station. There are high mountains behind the city. At a glance, you can tell that it is a place of strategic importance. Because I was eager to go to Puqi, I couldn't get off the train. I met a Xianning person in the train who talked about the situation in Xianning in great detail. The county is a third-class county with an area of 1,251 square kilometers, 125,404 mu of cultivated land, and a population of more than 140,000. The southeast is often dry, and the northwest suffers from waterlogging (now the water disaster has been reduced due to the completion of the Jinshui Dam). It has also suffered from banditry for a long time. Some of the land has been divided up. Security teams, strongmen teams, and anti-communist teams have all been organized. The security regiment's annual expenditure of 41,000 yuan is paid by the land, shops, tea, hemp, and paper donations, while the expenses of the armed strongmen team must be borne by the people themselves. At present, there are still remnants of bandits in the southwest, such as Baidun and Maqiao, and the areas bordering Yangquan and Banqiao in Puqi. Agricultural products are mainly paper, tea, and hemp. The paper mill produces 80,000 pieces of paper a year, worth 50,000 yuan; tea produces 30,000 dan, worth 200,000 yuan; and hemp produces 20,000 dan, worth more than 400,000 yuan. Recently, production has decreased, and sales have been sluggish. It is impossible for the people to make a living. I also asked about the situation of opium suppression and education. It is said that school education and social education are out of the question, and opium suppression still cannot avoid being relaxed, but there has been progress compared to the past.

At three o'clock in the afternoon, the train arrived at Tingshiqiao, which had entered Puqi. There, high mountains stand tall, and the atmosphere is magnificent. It is a vital road in the north and south, and a place that soldiers must contend for. In the fifteenth year of the Republic of China, the Revolutionary Army defeated Wu Peifu here. The fields were stained with blood, and the white bones supported the sky. When I look at it now, I can't help but feel sad about the wind and the sunset.

(2) Impressions of Puqi

I arrived in Beiqi at four o'clock on the 20th and stayed for two days. I got a lot of materials. The county is a first-class county. The first district administrative inspector is stationed here. The total county area is slightly over 158,025 square kilometers, the cultivated land is 225,053 mu, and the population is 181,640. It connects Xiang and Yue in the south and exits the Yangtze River in the west. It is a barrier to Wuhan. It was originally divided into five districts. The first district office was located in Xiangxiang, the second district office was located in Tingshiqiao, the third district office was located in Zhaoliqiao, the fourth district office was located in Chebu, and the fifth district office was located in Shenshan. Recently, it was changed to a district office and reduced to three districts. The first district office is located in the county seat, the second district office is located in Tingshiqiao, and the third district office is located in Xindian. Self-cultivating farmers account for 25%, tenant farmers account for 40%, and semi-self-cultivating farmers account for 35%. The largest products are tea, hemp, bamboo, and paper, which have always been famous. The people of Puqi like to boast about it. Yangloudong and Yanglousi are both tea-planting areas, producing more than 60,000 dan per year, which is a large output. Among agricultural products, rice produces more than 600,000 dan per year, hemp produces more than 5 million jin, and wheat, miscellaneous grains, and sweet potatoes produce a total of 50,000 dan per year. In addition to keeping grain for self-sufficiency, farmers can sell the rest, which is quite a joy to have a well-off family. In recent years, the Red Bandits have harassed the area, and the great drought in the previous year has exhausted the local vitality. The countryside is declining day by day. There is a large river in the county that originates in Tongshan, runs straight through the county seat, and enters the Yangtze River at Liuxikou. Every summer, mountain floods break out, and nearby fields and houses are flooded once. The people don't feel its pain, because mountain floods only affect the area near the river, and the whole county has a bumper harvest. In Puqi, there are nine years of rain and sunshine in ten years, and only one year suffers from drought. It can be said that it is blessed by nature, but most farmers are lazy and unwilling to work hard. If there is a major drought, they are too lazy to pump water for irrigation. In a good year, they waste the surplus on smoking and gambling. Therefore, although the land is fertile, the people are very poor. They do not know how to pay attention to water conservancy. Although the county river is not very harmful, the riverbed is getting higher day by day. In another ten years, the sand will reach half of the city. The people are indifferent to this. The ponds and dams in the villages are completely out of repair. Because there is a drought once every ten years, the ponds and dams lose their effectiveness. The people are lazy by nature, so why would they spend nine years of effort to save it for one year of use? And when there is a major drought in one year, there is no way to save it. During the great drought in the previous year, the government allocated deception work to repair the ponds. Huang Deyuan, the head of the second district, received 250 yuan, but only used 20 yuan to perfunctorily deal with it. The remaining 230 yuan was completely embezzled. Although it has been reported, it has not yet been concluded. It can be seen that the people of Puqi regard water conservancy as a child's play. It is no accident that agricultural production has decreased. Even tea, the main product, is declining day by day. At its peak, the Yangloudong tea garden produced 3 million catties per year, calculated at 16 taels per catty, and each catty was 9 yuan. Now it only produces more than 4 million small catties. There were 25 tea companies in the past, but now there are only 6 left. The nearby mountains, which used to be planted with tea trees and forests, are now bare. The burden on the people is not very heavy. In the past, the county government's expenses were insufficient, so it slightly collected tea donations, hemp industry shop donations, and fish industry shop donations, public security bureau shop donations, etc. to make up for it. Now they have all been abolished by the administrative commissioner's office. The mu donation is used to maintain security expenses, and one jiao is collected per mu. Compared with the eastern Hubei counties, which collect four or five jiao per mu, it is relatively light. But when I visited farmers' homes today, they still said that the mu donation was heavy, saying that it exceeded the regular tax. Because the regular tax has always been light, they feel that the mu donation is heavy. There is only one highway in the whole county. Bluestone roads are all over the county. They were all built by the people in the past. The county roads planned to be built are the Pu-Jia line, from Puqi to Jiayu, 30 kilometers long, and the Zhao-Xin line from Zhaoliqiao to Xindian, 12 kilometers long. It was decided to conscript labor to build them after the autumn farming season. Telephones from the county seat to Hongxia, from the county seat to Yangloudong, and from Yangquanfan to Tingshiqiao have all been erected and connected to calls, but the bamboo poles used as telephone poles are in danger of falling at any time. Education is not very developed. There is a junior high school in the county seat with three classes of students and three classes of attached complete elementary schools. There are only three complete elementary schools and 22 junior elementary schools in the villages. I visited the junior high school. Mr. Liang Ruilin, the principal of the school, led me to visit. The equipment is good, but the rest are simple and crude. Social education is almost non-existent. Only the county party department's civil education hall has remedial classes, which are only a symbolic addition. They are all in the county seat, and farmers have no chance to learn to read, so illiteracy accounts for 90% of the county. Opium has not yet been eradicated. The county seat, Xindian, and Shenshan all have Shicao shops, and it is said that there are still opium dens.

The county is adjacent to Xiang and Gan, and has suffered deeply from banditry in the past. The people of Tuqiao, Xiashan, Datian, Jingsha, Shiken, Yangquan, Hongshi, Xinxing, Yanglin, Baishi, Guantian, Longkeng, Xiaobai, Hongshan, and Doumen villages and towns were slaughtered by the communist bandits, and many died. At present, the First Army's Independent 35th Brigade and the Security Regiment are stationed in the county. Large groups of Red Bandits have disappeared, but sporadic small bandits, in groups of three or five, are still harassing everywhere. Recently, the Pingjiang banditry has become rampant again. A group is entrenched in Yaogushan, which borders four counties, and calls itself by the name of Xu Yangan. The people of Puqi then widely spread that Xu Bandit was not dead. The mountain where he is entrenched is pointed out by the people of Puqi from a distance to show it. The snow-covered peaks can still be vaguely seen. The people of the townships and towns have recently been ravaged by scattered bandits, and there are killings and injuries every day, and many have been kidnapped. They have come to the county seat to seek refuge, and spring plowing is almost abandoned. The only hope of the people is to eradicate the remaining bandits and stabilize order, and they have nothing else to ask for. I interviewed Chen Jicheng, the commander of the First Army and the commander-in-chief of the anti-banditry in the border area of Xiang, E, and Gan, and Yu Dian, the administrative commissioner of the First District, and had a long conversation with them. Chen said, "The three-province border area anti-banditry conference decided on a strategy, focusing on promoting politics and supplementing it with military affairs. At present, the remaining bandits take Pingjiang as their nest and roam the border area of Xiang and E. Although they are the old troops of Xu Yangan, Xu has indeed been captured and executed. The propaganda that Xu Bandit is still there is intended to frighten the people with false rumors. The result of the three-province anti-banditry conference is that I am also the commander of the anti-banditry in the First District and have the power to punish the civil officials in the district. Luo Lin is also the commander of the Second District and is stationed in Pingliu. Tan Daoyuan is the commander of the Third District and is stationed in Yichun. The troops are being concentrated separately and will start to encircle and suppress them immediately. At the latest, they can be eradicated within three months. It is decided to divide the anti-banditry into three steps. The first is the Qingxiang period, the second is the self-defense period, and the third is the Baojia period. After the bandits are cleared, we must promote politics with all our strength, and then we can have long-term peace and stability." Yu said, "At present, the only important policy is the four words of anti-banditry and pacifying the people. After the people live and work in peace and contentment, we will educate them and change their lazy customs. Although there are many other facilities, if they are not implemented well, they will disturb the people instead, and it is better to be quiet and do nothing." What the two said are all the urgent demands of the people, and it can be said that they are concise and to the point. The people of Puqi have a strong hope for anti-banditry. However, when there is a bandit alarm, they all hide it and do not report it. Even if they are subjected to official punishment, even being shot, they do not reveal a word. At first hearing, it is very contradictory, but the people of Puqi also have their own difficulties. In the past, when official troops and teams suppressed bandits, the people were happy to guide them, and there were those who tied up bandits to offer them. But as a result, the whole family would be killed by the bandits, and the government would not provide any protection. Moreover, if they reported the bandits' tracks, they would be detained first. If the bandits had left, they would be accused of spreading rumors. If the suppression failed, they would be falsely accused of being bandit spies. Later, it became a common practice. It is better to be ravaged by the Red Bandits than to report to the government. Chen's troops moved here from Daye, and the soldiers and civilians are still harmonious. However, the people are very dissatisfied with Li Zongjian's troops of the Independent 35th Brigade. It is said that the discipline of this unit is the worst in the country. Although some say it is an exaggeration, it is an indisputable fact that this unit does not care about the population.

When I visited the eastern township, I heard two things that made people feel unhappy. Hongxia in the eastern township is 40 li away from the city and is the border between Chongyang and Puqi. Two platoons of Li's troops are stationed there, one platoon leader is Hu Liangxian, and the other is Li Yuhe. They are both stationed in the house of Liu Maorong, who runs a paper shop. Liu's son, Mei Cai, married a woman named Sanyuan, who is young and beautiful. Hu and Li often made fun of her, causing her to be humiliated. On the nineteenth day of the first lunar month, Li Zailin and Li Changbao, shop assistants in Liu's shop, introduced four people from Pingjiang, including Li Qisheng, to work in the shop. Each carried a good citizen certificate issued by Pingjiang County. Hu, angry because of the humiliation, arrested Li Qisheng and the other four, subjected them to torture, and forced them to confess to being bandits. The Baozhang went to bail them out and was also detained. When Li Qisheng's family and the local Lianbao director and Baojia chiefs came to Puqi to rescue them on the 20th of this month, Li Qisheng and the other four had been shot. They had to take the corpses back to Xiang. Sanyuan was then raped and occupied by Hu. The other incident also happened in Hongxia. Two brothers were rowing a boat together. The elder brother rowed the boat away, and the younger brother went to look for them. It happened that Li's Brigade was suppressing bandits and arrested him. He was also beaten severely. Later, he was bailed out by the Chamber of Commerce and was able to save his life. If this is the case, it will be difficult for the soldiers and civilians to get along, and the future of anti-banditry will be greatly affected. I have not been to Hongxia, and I secretly hope that what I have said is not true. (Sent from Puqi on the 22nd)

Japanese Establish Salt Industry Company in Changchun 84

Will Monopolize the Export of Industrial Salt to Japan

The Pseudo-Government Invests More Than 620,000 Yuan

Changchun News: Regarding the establishment of the "Manchuria" Salt Industry Company, which has been a pending issue, the Japanese operators have consulted with the pseudo-organization and held a meeting in the Kwantung Army. Under the participation of the Kwantung Army Staff Department, the pseudo-organization General Affairs Office, the pseudo-Finance Department, the pseudo-Industry Department, and the South Manchuria Railway (Mantetsu) related operators, based on the establishment outline, the company law, the business plan, and other issues were finally consulted. Based on the outline, the company law will be formulated at the end of March, and the establishment general meeting will be held in pseudo-Xinjing in early April. Among the capital of 5 million yuan, the first installment of 2.5 million yuan will be paid, and the pseudo-organization will invest 625,000 yuan. As for the company's salt production, it will be 150,000 tons per year, all of which will be industrial salt and will be exclusively exported to Japan. Its business will be monopolized by Japan. (Northeast News Agency)

Measures to Aid Anhui Tea Production: Banks Provide Loans of 500,000 Yuan 85

Qimen Establishes Improvement Center, Reduces Transportation Costs, and Improves Communication in Yanhu. Anhui tea, renowned both domestically and internationally, has been affected by the overall decline of the rural economy on tea farmers. Coupled with adherence to outdated practices and a failure to innovate, this has led to a sharp decline in production. Foreign trade has also steadily declined. According to preliminary statistics from the Anhui Provincial Tea Business Tax Bureau, exports for the 24th year of the Republic (1935) totaled only 179,479 dan. Within this, the Huizhou region, including Shexian, Xiuning, and Qimen counties, accounted for more than two-thirds of the total. The National Economic Council, concerned that Anhui tea's position in the international market would be encroached upon by Indian and Ceylon tea if improvements and aid were not urgently implemented, convened the Ministry of Industry and the Anhui Provincial Government to establish a large-scale tea improvement center in Qimen, hoping to achieve tangible results. However, given the economic situation of tea farmers, aid was still necessary. Recently, the provincial government dispatched Duan Tianjue, a technician from the Construction Department, and Hu Shiqi, a chief clerk from the Finance Department, together with Hu Haochuan, director of the Qimen Tea Improvement Committee of the National Economic Council, to Shanghai to negotiate loans with the banking sector. The Bank of Communications agreed to cooperate with the Anhui Local Bank to provide a total of 500,000 yuan in production loans for Anhui tea. The Bank of Communications will provide 400,000 yuan, and the Anhui Local Bank will provide 100,000 yuan. The loan measures are divided into three categories: loan introduction, cooperative societies, and transportation and sales loans, which will be handled separately based on the urgency of their needs. Personnel have already been dispatched to Qimen to establish an office and begin preparations. The Anhui Construction Department has specifically instructed the Anhui-Hefei, Provincial-Tunxi, and Wuhu-Tunxi highway vehicle management offices to reduce tea transportation rates to third-class rates as the tea market season approaches. The standard rate for third-class goods is set at six cents per quarter ton, according to the freight rates of five provinces and cities, to facilitate transportation. (March 23)

Jingxing Coal Sales Affected by Shanxi Military Actions 86

Coal Stocks Along the Pinghan Railway Sold Out

Beijing Correspondence: The Jingxing Coal Mine has been significantly affected in its transportation due to the war in Shanxi. Coal prices in the north have increased, and future market prices will be even higher. Gu Zhongxiu, Chairman of the Hebei Provincial Industry Supervision Committee, came to Beijing on the 15th to meet with Song Zheyuan. According to Gu's conversation, "The Jingxing Coal Mine was originally privately exploited by Germans. When the Chinese government became aware of this, a Sino-German joint venture was implemented. It was briefly taken back during World War I but then restored to its original status. Since the provincial government implemented supervision, production has increased even more. Recently, daily coal production has been around 3,000 tons, with a record high of 3,200 tons, an achievement unseen in decades. The Zhengtai Railway Bureau provides ten trains daily to transport coal out of the mine, selling it throughout North China. Business is very prosperous. Monthly revenue can reach 480,000 to 490,000 yuan during peak season, and over 300,000 yuan during off-peak months. Currently, the total assets of the mine have reached 11 million yuan. The initial capital was only 300,000 taels, which shows the speed of its development. However, the railway connecting the mine to the Zhengtai Railway, originally built by the mine, has narrower tracks than the Zhengtai Railway. Therefore, daily coal transportation requires coal cars from the mine to be unloaded into coal cars on the Zhengtai Railway, which is not economical in terms of labor and time. Recently, the Mining Supervision Committee decided to build a new railway line, moving the location to Weishui, which would shorten the route by two kilometers. The construction cost is 500,000 yuan, which will be drawn from the Jingxing Mine's surplus. Construction has not yet begun. Recently, due to military action in Shanxi, there are more military trains on the Zhengtai Railway. The Zhengtai Railway Bureau can only allocate five or six trains daily to transport coal. Therefore, the daily coal supply to various places is not enough to meet sales needs. Currently, coal stocks along the Pinghan Railway have been sold out, and prices are bound to rise. However, recent victories in the war in the west are expected to restore coal transportation on the Zhengtai Railway to its original state within days, and this situation should be alleviated."

"After the Lincheng Coal Mine was flooded, the mine conducted several surveys and concluded that the cost of dewatering would exceed the potential gains from mining. Therefore, it was decided to abandon it and open a new mine in Cixian. This plan has also been approved, but work has not yet begun. After the closure of the Lincheng Mine, all procedures were completed. A recent report stated that 50,000 yuan was still owed in wages to employees. This was owed by the previous business operation, before 1925. The mine was operated by a company organized by Li [blank space] and others. Later, due to poor performance, it was taken over by the provincial government. At that time, the merchants reported losses of tens of millions of yuan, most of which were false. In reality, the losses were minimal, and this has been clarified. There was already 50,000 yuan owed to employees at that time. Over time, many of the old workers were replaced. After the provincial government took over, employee wages were paid monthly, but the old debts were never addressed. This is the origin of the old workers' demand for repayment of the outstanding debts. The Hebei Province's new village resettlement program has been performing well in the past. This year, resettlement will continue. Recently, a suitable location was found in the Xiwuli area of Baotou, Suiyuan. The soil is very fertile and can accommodate more than 600 households. It has been decided to build a new village there. This plan has been approved by the Hebei Provincial Government, but the actual situation still needs to be considered due to economic factors."

Zhongdetang Pharmacy Destroyed by Fire 88

Zhongdetang Pharmacy on Beida Street in the city caught fire in the rear workshop at about 3:00 AM on the 23rd. The people in the store were sound asleep and no one noticed, so the fire became very intense. The roof was quickly burned through. By the time they got up and cried for help, it was impossible to put out the fire. The fire brigade arrived after being alerted, but the workshop was completely burned down. The store was filled with medicinal materials, all of which were reduced to ashes. The estimated loss is seven or eight hundred yuan.

Suzhou: The Provincial Silver Union Holds Annual Meeting Again in Suzhou

The Jiangsu Provincial Goldsmiths' Union held its annual meeting yesterday (the 24th) at the Lijegong Office of the Goldsmiths' Association in Liujia Bang, Jinmen, Suzhou. More than 30 representatives from various counties, including Zhenjiang, Wuxi, Wujin, Aoyang, Kunshan, Songjiang, Taiyu, Ru, and Jiangdu, including Xiang Ziqiao, Wang Zisun, and Wang Hongbin, attended. A preparatory meeting was held in the morning. At noon, the Wuxian Goldsmiths' Association hosted a banquet for the representatives of the various counties. The official meeting began at 2:00 PM. Representatives from five counties, including Zhenjiang, Wuxian, Jiangdu, Wuxi, and Dongtai, were elected as the presidium. Cai Jilun, chairman of the presidium, gave an opening address and reported on the efforts to address the silver fineness issue. They had repeatedly resolved to jointly fight for a favorable outcome with representatives from various regions to the government, but had not yet achieved their goals. Subsequently, representatives from various counties expressed their opinions, unanimously stating that if the government's prescribed method of using 30% silver and 70% impurities were followed for silver jewelry, the industry would be ruined and the livelihoods of tens of thousands of employees would be threatened, making a vigorous fight essential. After discussion, seven people were selected as a delegation: Cai Jilun from Zhenjiang, Zhang Shanqing from Wuxi, Cheng Shuli from Wuxian, Zhuge Shenfu from Dongtai, Xiang Zigao from Jiangdu, Zhu Shouhe from Taixing, and Su Caifan from Changshu. They will join representatives from the three cities of Shanghai, Nanjing, and Hankou, as well as the same trade from Zhejiang Province, to present the various difficulties and petition the Central Party Headquarters and various departments and ministries of the National Government, striving to achieve the goal of still using 100% silver for silver jewelry, to maintain the livelihoods of tens of thousands of workers in the trade. The meeting then adjourned. Some representatives left Suzhou that evening, while others will visit Dengwei Mountain in Guangfu Township today (the 25th) to view the plum blossoms.

Jiangsu and Zhejiang Water Police Encircling Bandits on Taihu Lake

Winter defense has passed, and banditry on Taihu Lake has arisen. Robberies are frequently reported in villages around the lake. A large group of lake bandits specializing in robbery has recently been discovered in the Xinkai River area of Nantai Lake, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. It is now learned that Zhou Weilie, director of the Second Water Security District, reported that this group of lake bandits numbers over 100 and is well-equipped with firearms. It is also known that Zhejiang Province water police have also departed from Wuxing County to Taihu Lake to jointly encircle and suppress the bandits, hoping to quickly eliminate the lake bandits and maintain security in the rural areas.

Wuxi: Implementation of Urban Household Land Survey

The Jiangsu Provincial Government had previously determined that land in various counties urgently needed to be surveyed and reorganized. Therefore, it first carried out urban land price declarations and aerial surveys in Wuxi and Nantong counties. By the end of last year, both had been completed with good results. The County Land Bureau is now handling registration separately. However, urban land is densely packed with houses, and the terrain is complex, which cannot be handled by aerial surveys. Therefore, the Provincial Government specially ordered the Provincial Land Bureau to dispatch an urban land surveying team to Wuxi in January of this year. The team established a traverse line group in Guanqian Street in the city center and began surveying the streets, alleys, and lanes. Work within the city walls has now been completed and is progressing towards the urban areas outside the city. The team leader, Xue Gansheng, and his staff arrived in Wuxi from Suzhou the day before yesterday to prepare for the urban household land survey. It is also heard that the Provincial Land Bureau has ordered a large number of excellent surveyors who were surveying urban areas in Wuxian County to come to Wuxi soon to carry out the household survey.

Case of Gangster Beating Detective Transferred to Shanghai

Cai Jianchun from Taixing, a worker at a public stove in the Shenxiang area of the city, had an affair with Zhang Shao, a woman from Changshu. They were very intimate and planned to live together permanently. On the 15th of last month, they hired Shi Haishan from Yancheng to write a document at the Wan'an Inn. A patrol officer from the First Public Security Bureau arrived at the inn for inspection and found their behavior suspicious. Upon inspection, a diary was found on Shi Haishan containing the phrases "Gao Yusheng killed detective Lu Guiqing at Chenjia Bridge, South Wharf, Shanghai," etc. Considering the situation serious, the three men and women were sent to the General Bureau and then to the court for interrogation and detention. Now, the Shanghai Municipal Public Security Bureau, after learning of the above case, specially ordered Squad Leader Liu Bingyuan of the Detective Team to come to Wuxi with a document yesterday to greet and transfer them from the court. Director Liu of the court ordered Shi to be brought to court for questioning before handing him over to Liu to transfer him to Shanghai for further investigation.

Trial of Teacher-Student Affair Begins

Jiu Fen, wife of Sun Zhonghao from Shitangwan in the Tenth District, was a teacher at Kangjiawan Tangwan Elementary School in the Laoximen area of Shanghai. She had an affair with student Chen Lin. On the 10th of this month, Chen Lin came to Wuxi from Shanghai and met with Jiu Fen in a private room at the Shenjiang Hotel on Tonghui Road. Her husband, Sun Zhonghao, discovered this and called the police, who arrested the adulterer and adulteress and sent them to the court for interrogation and detention. After investigation, Prosecutor Shen filed a public lawsuit against them for adultery under Article 239 of the Criminal Law. Yesterday (the 24th) morning at 10:00 AM, the first public hearing of the case was held. The defendant hired lawyer Tang Ying to appear in court for defense. Judge Liu Bingzhen opened the court and first questioned Chen Lin, who stated that he was 20 years old, from Shanghai, and that his relationship with Lu Jiu Fen was that of a teacher and a foster mother, and that they did not have an adulterous relationship. He admitted that they had talked in the room. Judge then questioned Sun Lu Jiu Fen, who stated that she was 32 years old, from Shitangwan, Wuxi, and that she was formerly a teacher and is now at home. "Chen Lin and I are indeed teacher and foster mother. The teahouse waiter at the Shenjiang Hotel said that Chen Lin and I stayed for four or five days. This was entirely fabricated by the plaintiff. In June of last year, the plaintiff asked me for an unconditional divorce, which I did not agree to. His sister's affairs in Shanghai have nothing to do with him. If there is anything disreputable, he can report it to the police for investigation." She completely denied the adultery. Next, Sun Zhonghao stated that he was 33 years old, from Shitangwan, and an office worker at the Dahua Paint Factory in Longhua, Shanghai. "Lu Jiu Fen is my wife. We have been married for over ten years. At first, we respected each other as husband and wife. Later, after she had an affair with Chen Lin (also known as Chen Shiming), she left a letter and ran away from Shanghai on September 18th of last year, and paid 100 yuan at the exchange to flee to Mu Du, Suzhou. I went to find her and persuaded her to go home, but she did not agree. At this point, I was extremely heartbroken. As this case involves morality, I request the judge to investigate it severely," and so on. At this point, the clock struck twelve, and Judge Liu adjourned until 2:00 PM to continue the trial. First, Sun Zhonghao was questioned, then Chen Lin and Jiu Fen. Finally, lawyer Tang Ying came out to defend Chen Lin. The trial ended at about 4:00 PM. The audience was very crowded, reaching over 200 people. As a result of the court hearing, Lu Jiu Fen was released on bail, guaranteed by the Hengda Watch & Glasses Company on Tongyun Road and Hu Zaiping. Sun Zhonghao was ordered to return home, and Chen Lin was returned to custody to await review.

Those present at the meeting yesterday afternoon included Li Yuxuan of the Guangdong Native Place Association, Wu Rulin of the Money Trade Association, Ye Jia and Liu Zhongying and Zhang Yiqing of the Citizens' Federation, Xu Jichang and Fang Jiaobo of the Taxpayers' Association, Dong Xinqin of the Ningbo Native Place Association, Cao Zhigong of the Huining Native Place Association, Qian Youlan of the Shaoxing Native Place Association, Zheng Dongshan of the Citizens' Association for National Goods, Jin Runxiang of the Municipal Chamber of Commerce, Hu Fengxiang of the Citizens' National Goods Year Association, Lin Kanghou of the Bankers' Association, Gu Wensheng of the Pudong Native Place Association, Zhu Zhichun and Huang Guicheng of the Municipal Federation Branch, and 17 others. The written report of Chairman Xu Jiching regarding the investigation stated: "In this election, in addition to publishing notices in newspapers and soliciting taxpayers to come to the association to fill out forms, the association also pre-filled the names of taxpayers in the survey form based on the membership list of the previous session, and then sent personnel to conduct investigations separately. If there were no changes, it remained the same, and the taxpayer only needed to stamp the survey form to prove it. If there were any changes, it was filled out separately. By the end of December of last year, a total of 7,487 old and new survey forms were received, and 2,842 survey forms were sent by various groups, totaling 10,329. Before compiling the roster, after excluding duplicates and those who did not meet the requirements, the actual number was 9,672. Therefore, the draft number of the election roster was 9,672. After the investigation was completed, the election roster was compiled, with and without the right to be elected. On March 8, it was announced in the newspaper in accordance with election conventions. After compiling the draft number of the electors' name roster, four duplicates and three deceased people were found again, so the actual number was only 9,665. Among them, 6,120 had the right to vote, and 3,545 also had the right to be elected. Therefore, the election roster's official number is 6,665, and the number of election ballots issued in Shanghai is 9,665, which matches the above numbers. Please refer to the investigation statistics table. Also, after the election ballot numbers were determined, electors He Zhongxiao, number 376, and Li Jueshan, number 941, passed away, so the election ballots for those numbers were stopped from being issued. Therefore, the total number of ballots actually issued was 9,663. This is combined and stated on March 24, 25th year of the Republic of China.

River Water in Sichuan Rising: Passenger Transport Now Possible 94

The Shanghai steamer that departed yesterday evening for the upper reaches of the Yangtze River, above Yichang, had been unable to navigate the Sichuan river route because the water level had dropped to just two inches above the riverbed. This matter was previously reported in this newspaper. Recently, the water level has slightly risen, and passenger steamers can now barely make their way to Chongqing. A ship also departed from Shanghai yesterday. The detailed situation is described below.

Fuyang First to Enter Sichuan: The Sanbei Company's Sichuan River steamer Fuyang was forced to stop downstream of Yichang due to the shallow water levels in the upper reaches. It was unable to pass through the shallow waters and remained anchored for over ten days. More than ten other Chinese and foreign merchant steamers were also stranded. Yesterday, this newspaper received a telegram from Yichang stating that the water level in the upper river was gradually rising and that with a south wind, it would rise further, allowing navigation. The Sanbei Fuyang has already loaded passengers (without carrying goods) and set off for Chongqing as the first to go. It has already passed through the shallowest areas.

Guangyao Departs Shanghai with Cargo: The Minsheng Company also received a telegram from Sichuan yesterday stating that the upper river was rising and navigable for a short period of time. A large amount of cargo has accumulated in Shanghai, and there is a great need in Sichuan. The company was ordered to load cargo first. Therefore, the company began loading passengers and cargo onto the Guangyao steamer yesterday to enter Sichuan. It is hoped that the river water will have risen by the time the ship arrives in Yichang, allowing the steamer to enter Sichuan. If the water level has not risen, then a portion of the cargo will be unloaded when it arrives in Yichang, and then it will sail upstream.

National Mining Association Cables Request to Cancel Coal Tax in Guangdong 100

Release Shipments with Ministry of Finance Licenses to Maintain the Mining Industry

The National Mining Association of China, in response to the Guangdong Provincial Department of Finance's collection of a tax on imported coal, cabled the Guangdong authorities yesterday to immediately cancel the tax and release shipments upon verification of the tax-paid licenses issued by the Ministry of Finance in order to maintain the mining industry. The original cable stated, "To the Guangdong Provincial Government and the Department of Finance: Regarding the tax on domestic coal, the Ministry of Finance has established uniform measures, dispatching personnel to the mines to collect the tax and issue tax-paid licenses, without imposing additional taxes. However, your province has issued an order, effective from January 27th of this year, imposing a coal tax of 50 cents per ton on imported coal, which is collected by the Local Agricultural Products Miscellaneous Special Tax Bureau. This has caused great alarm among the mines. This illegal and excessive tax not only violates the national unified tax system and hinders the mines' sales prospects but also undermines the provincial plan. Guangdong's coal production is limited and relies entirely on coal from other provinces. The excessive coal tax will reduce imports and impede the province's industrial and commercial enterprises. We request that you consider this and immediately cancel the tax. All imported coal should be released tax-free upon verification of the tax-paid license issued by the Ministry of Finance in order to maintain the mining industry," Chairman Wang Zhengting.
