Suggestions from Executive Committee Members Ye Jiaxing and Others of the Ratepayers' Association: Cease Interference with the Collection of Aviation Donations: Leaseholds Not Comparable to Colonies; A Strong Protest Should Be Made Based on Reason 103

Due to the interference by the Shanghai Municipal Council with the collection of donations for aviation and national salvation, Executive Committee members Ye Jiaxing and Gu Wensheng of the Chinese Ratepayers' Association of the Public Leasehold yesterday proposed a serious negotiation to cease the interference. The original proposal is recorded below. "The authorities of the Shanghai Public Leasehold and the French Leasehold have recently and abruptly prevented the collection of aviation donations in hotels within the two special districts and have confiscated all receipts and account books, or even revoked business licenses. The extent of their imposition of pressure and suppression of patriotic movements has reached an extreme. If this can be tolerated, what cannot be tolerated? It is requested that the Association argue the case based on reason and conduct a serious negotiation." The reasons are attached below for discussion. "(Reasons) The opening of the Leaseholds is not comparable to colonies, and the citizens within the Leaseholds are definitely not residents of colonies. In other words, the citizens within the Leaseholds have their own absolute autonomy and can absolutely express their patriotic feelings. Therefore, the collection of aviation donations by the hotel industry, etc., within the two Leaseholds is a citizen's duty to their country and should not be interfered with by the Leasehold administrative authorities. Moreover, at the beginning of the collection, our government followed diplomatic practice and assisted the two Leaseholds, and the Leasehold authorities expressed their agreement. Now, they have suddenly prevented it, which is not only contradictory but also treats the people's voluntary aviation donation movement as a child's play. The national character of our Republic of China still exists. Therefore, this Association, as the representative spokesperson for the Chinese ratepayers within the Leaseholds, should argue the case based on reason and conduct a serious negotiation until the goal of continuing to collect is achieved. This is our opinion, and we respectfully request a decision."

China Merchants Steam Navigation Company to Abolish the Compradore System Starting April 1st: Office Managers to be Established, Tea Boys to be Renamed Service Staff, Military Police Assigned to Check Tickets Ashore, Cracking Down on Fare Evasion, Setting Fares for Poor Passengers 104

The state-run China Merchants Steam Navigation Company is scheduled to abolish the compradore system starting April 1st, to establish office managers, to rename tea boys as service staff, and to have military police check tickets, strictly prohibit fare evasion. Detailed information is recorded below.

Decision to Improve Business Methods 105

In addition to holding qualification examinations for staff at the head office and branch offices, the Ministry of Communications is reorganizing the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company and convened a meeting of business directors of various steamers on the 22nd to improve business operations. Business directors Zhang Yanling and others, as well as General Manager Cai Zengji, Business Section Chief Shi Yixuan, and General Affairs Section Chief Wang Xiangchen, all went to Beijing to participate in the meeting. Acting Minister Yu Feipeng presided over the meeting and decided on concrete measures to improve business operations. General Manager Cai and the business directors left Beijing on the evening of the 23rd and returned to Shanghai on the morning of the 24th.

Implementation of Abolishing the Compradore System 106

The abolition of the compradore system is scheduled to be implemented on April 1st. Office managers will be established on each steamer, and salaries will be provided by the company. Ticket purchases ashore are required. Six military police officers will be assigned to each steamer to escort the ship and check tickets. Fare evasion will be strictly prohibited. Tea boys will be thoroughly reorganized and renamed as service staff. Wages will be provided by the company. Strict measures will be taken to prohibit the solicitation of tips from passengers. At the same time, to show compassion for poor passengers, fares for poor passengers will be established. The service staff on each steamer will undergo new life training.

Starting with Yangtze River Steamers 107

The China Merchants Steam Navigation Company will implement the abolition of the compradore system on April 1st, starting with the steamers on the Yangtze River route. A list of the names of the steamers on the Yangtze River route and the names of the business directors is recorded below: Jianghua Zhang Yanling, Jiangshun Jin Tingsun, Jiang'an Zhou Da'wu, Jiangxin Liu Jida, Jianguo Shen Yougeng, Kuaili Shen Huating, Jiangda Zhang Zhongyu. The business directors will be renamed office managers. However, the Jiangjing steamer has already abolished the compradore system, and the office manager is Huan Chaoying.

Qualification Examinations Nearing Completion 108

After the announcement of the results of the qualification examinations at the head office, Business Section staff member Yun Zhi ranked first in the examinations, but he has now been dismissed. Other dismissed employees include radio engineer Fang Ziwei and several others. In addition, the Ministry approved the appointment of Chen Shaoji as the Chief of the Shipping Section and Zhou Houkun as the Deputy Chief. As for the qualification examinations at the branch offices in various locations, after Deputy Manager Tan Boying was dispatched to preside over them, they are nearing completion. After being submitted to the Ministry of Communications, decisions on retention and dismissal will be made.

The Xin Jiangtian Case Reopened for Arbitration Yesterday: Testimony Taken from Chen Tianxiao 109

The case of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company's Xin Jiangtian steamer colliding with and sinking the civilian ship Jin Wanli at Yawo Shoal has already been decided by the Collision Arbitration Committee. However, because the testimony of the Jin Wanli boatman Chen Tianxiao had not yet been taken, the arbitrators convened again yesterday afternoon to question him. Chen Tianxiao's testimony is recorded below. Chen Tianxiao, from Huangyan, 40 years old, boatman, 10 years of experience, only started as Jin Wanli boatman last year, always travelling the Shanghai-Wenzhou route. Departed from Wusong at 3:00 AM on the 18th. The sky was dark, but very clear. Wind direction, northeast wind. Tide, at half-tide. Exited along the southern foot of the inner buoy. Steamed with the compass heading east by south. Saw the buoys on the water. Did not see the buoy ahead. After passing the black buoy, saw a ship at anchor about two li ahead. Saw the red and white lights of the approaching ship, directly in front of our ship, and immediately paid attention. After steaming for another li, to be safe, we slightly turned our rudder, but suddenly saw the red and green lights of the approaching ship, and it immediately collided with our ship. The wooden ship's lamp was placed on the left side of the cabin, about one person high from the boat. There was only one lamp on the boat. There were two people on the bow looking out. The bow of the Xin Jiangtian collided with the bow of our ship on the left side. The bow of our ship immediately sank after the collision. I was on the ship and put down the sampan. There were eight people in total in the stern. All eight people jumped onto the sampan. Two people were on the bow and fell into the water immediately after the collision, I did not see them. One person was in the cabin and did not have time to jump onto the sampan, so he was drowned. I never heard the Xin Jiangtian pull back. There were no oars on the sampan. Later, we drifted by wind to Wangjiawan, Pudong. The US Consulate General is reportedly relocating from the old Hotel Cleyer location to the newly completed high-rise building at the corner of Fuzhou Road and Jiangxi Road. The relocation began yesterday. The Office of the US Treasury Department in China will be the first to move in, followed by the US Court for China. All actions are very rapid, so it is expected that all three agencies can begin operations in the new building by next Monday.

China Agricultural Banking Syndicate: Successful Trial Operation in 1935; Total Loans of One Million Yuan; Expansion Sought This Year Through Cooperation 113

The China Agricultural Lending Syndicate completed its operations for the 1935 fiscal year, with total loans of one million yuan, achieving excellent results. This fiscal year, it plans to seek cooperation with various banks for expansion. Details are recorded below.

Completion of Last Year's Agricultural Loans 114

The Agricultural Lending Syndicate is a joint venture of ten banks: Bank of Communications, Bank of Shanghai, Zhejiang Industrial Bank, Jin City Bank, New China Bank, Central China Bank, Continental Bank, Guohua Bank, Chinese Farmers' Bank, and the Four Banks Savings Association. Agricultural lending for the 1935 fiscal year has been completed and is scheduled to be finalized by the end of the month. The loans are divided into production, transportation, and beneficial uses, with the area being Shanxi, Hebei, Henan, and Shanxi provinces.

Trial Operation Proves Effective 115

In the 1935 fiscal year, the total agricultural loan amount was one million yuan, with 50% for production loans, 40% for transportation loans, and 10% for beneficial use loans. Cotton accounted for 90% of the loans, while wheat and other crops accounted for 10%. The annual interest rate was set at 9%. The loans released have been gradually recovered, with excellent results. Last year was the first year of the syndicate's establishment, and it was a trial operation that has proven effective.

Decision to Expand This Year 116

The banks participating in the syndicate, in view of the excellent results last year, have decided to continue their participation and seek cooperation with other banks to expand. It is reported that after the completion of last year's operations, cooperation will be sought, and a general meeting will be convened to elect directors and discuss lending methods. The total loan amount and the geographical scope will be expanded.

Shipping Industry Association Investigates General Conditions of Vessel Freight 117

The Shanghai Shipping Industry Association has issued a notice to various shipping companies, stating, "It has been noted that advanced shipping nations in the West conduct detailed investigations into various aspects of their national vessels and publish them in various magazines for reference. All companies engaged in the shipping industry also provide as much information as possible for reporting purposes in order to develop shipping and improve operations. In the Far East, countries such as Japan have seen a rapid increase in the number of ships and a thriving shipping industry in recent years. The reason for this is due to the government's support and effective management. Information on maritime transport, materials, and market conditions for goods has never been considered confidential. The "Marine Transport" and "Marine Transport Statistics Monthly Report" published by the Japan Maritime Transport Association are detailed and contribute to the promotion of the shipping industry. In contrast, there is very little reference to such records in China, which hinders the shipping industry. In light of this, the Association has printed a "Vessel Freight Overview Investigation Table" and will begin by investigating the freight transport situation of vessels without fixed routes in order to compile statistics and publish them in the Shipping Monthly to promote publicity and development. We are sending you a copy of the investigation table and request that you fill it out with the freight rates of all ships owned or represented by your company from January 1st of this year and return it to the Association for compilation. We greatly appreciate your cooperation." The Vessel Freight Overview Investigation Table includes: Vessel Name, Goods Transported (by type and quantity), Loading Date, Route, Freight Charges, Vessel User (Owner, Agent, Charterer), and Remarks.

The United Factories Association Requests Guangdong Province to Exempt Rubber Shoe Tax 118

The Shanghai United Association of Machine-Made National Product Factories yesterday submitted a request to the Guangdong Provincial Finance Department to exempt the minor rubber shoe tax. The original text stated, "Submitting this request for machine-made national products, urging the conversion to exemption of imported goods tax, in order to benefit national products." The letter from member Zhengtian Xinji Rubber Factory stated, "Recently, we received a letter from Shantou Hakka Dingda Firm stating that the Guangdong Provincial Finance Department has established a special tax bureau for imported agricultural products and miscellaneous items within the province, and rubber-soled cloth shoes imported from outside the province are also handled according to this regulation, with a tax of five cents per pair, or sixty cents per dozen, about to be levied. Please negotiate reasonably to reduce the burden," etc. According to the factory, the "Daxi" and "Huili" brand rubber-soled cloth shoes manufactured by our factory are sold throughout Guangdong. If a heavy tax of sixty cents per dozen is levied, the impact will inevitably lead to zero sales of our factory's products. Moreover, this regulation was originally designed to resist imported goods, so it specifically targets imports. It is incomprehensible that it now affects national products. Furthermore, Shanghai and Guangdong are both territories of the Republic of China. How can imports and national products from outside the province be equated? If our factory's rubber-soled cloth shoes are taxed because the rubber belongs to imports, then Guangzhou's cloth-surface rubber-soled shoes should also be taxed as imported goods based on their rubber, in order to be fair. Otherwise, it would inevitably be biased. This matter concerns the development of national products. We request your association to appeal on our behalf, and we would be extremely grateful," etc. Upon investigation by the association, the "Daxi" and "Huili" brand rubber-soled cloth shoes produced by Zhengtian Xinji Rubber Factory are indeed machine-made national products and are exempt from imported miscellaneous taxes. Therefore, we specifically submit this request, hoping that your department will review and approve it, ordering the Shantou Special Tax Bureau and other special tax bureaus to uniformly exempt the tax, which would be of public benefit.

Last Year's Tung Oil Export Statistics: Value Over 41.1 Million, Totaling Over 738,000 Metric Tons 119

According to the International Trade Bureau's statistics, the total export of tung oil nationwide last year was 738,865 metric tons, with a value of 41,158,270 yuan in national currency. This is an increase of 86,029 metric tons compared to the previous year. However, according to the bureau's information, the export volume last year was still less than that of 1933, and the value was also less than that of 1930. Tung oil is a unique product of our country and has a monopoly in the world market. Currently, only the United States is experimenting with tung tree planting. If improvements can be made, such as increasing oil production and improving packaging, attention should be paid to these aspects.

Respectfully submitted to the Mayor of the Shanghai Municipal Government."

Eastern Youheng Road: Morphine Den Busted 123

Addicts Receive Varying Sentences

Korean Women Handed Over to Japanese Consulate

Fougen, a Western detective from the Jiading Road Police Station, along with Chinese detective Dong Qingquan and officer No. 3158, discovered that someone was secretly selling morphine and opium substitutes in a house at No. 122, Eastern Youheng Road, making a considerable profit. They rushed to the address and arrested the suspects on the night of the incident, where they found several addicts lying on couches, indulging in opium smoking. Ding Guixi from Zhenjiang and Jiang Caigen, along with eight others, were arrested. A Korean woman sitting on the side was identified by the addicts as the "boss." The woman admitted to the accusation, and thirty small packets of morphine were found on her person. Soon after, another Korean woman entered the premises. The Chinese and Western detectives took both Korean women, along with the opium lamps and smoking pipes, back to the police station. The police chief ordered the two women to be handed over to the Japanese consulate. Ding Guixi and the others were brought before the Third Criminal Court of the First Special District Court yesterday morning. Zhang Shizhu, the lawyer for the Shanghai Municipal Council, presented the case, and the Chinese and Western detectives explained the details of the arrest. After examining the evidence, Judge Xiao Bianfen questioned the defendants thoroughly. After appointing lawyer Chen Zhen to defend Ding Guixi and the others, the court sentenced Ding Guixi, Xu Amao, Wang Agen, and Wang Shuangtu to two years of imprisonment each, and Xu Jinsheng, Ma Laoer, Chen Azhang, and Zhou Chaojia to one year and six months of imprisonment each. All were to be sent to an anti-addiction hospital for one month of rehabilitation before serving their sentences. The evidence was confiscated. Yuan Yongcai and Jiang Caigen were acquitted and released.

Japanese Resident: Suicide Due to Heartbreak 124

Suicide Note States Lack of Interest in Life

Heartless Woman Shortens a Man's Life: According to the Japanese newspaper "Riri Nichinichi Shimbun," Kawatachu Yuuxio, a clerk at a foreign firm on Haining Road from Nara Prefecture, had dinner with his boss last night. He was drunk and depressed. He went to a Japanese coffee shop on Hongjiang Road. A waitress named Takako, with whom Kawatachu had a relationship, was there. They drank coffee together until 11 p.m., then Kawatachu said goodbye to Takako and went alone to his boss's factory. He obtained a heavy amount of chromic acid, mixed it with ten grams of hydrochloric acid, and ingested it. Factory workers discovered the incident and rushed him to Fukumin Hospital. Fortunately, the time was short, and his life was not in danger. After investigating the cause of Kawatachu's suicide, it was found that Takako's attitude towards him had become cold recently, which led to his despair. A suicide note was found in his pocket, stating, "I have lacked interest in life for three years, and a heartless woman shortens a man's life," and other words.

Wang Jisheng Swallows Potassium Cyanide out of Fear of Losing His Job 125

Died En Route to the Hospital

Yesterday, the body was examined by the court and handed over to his mother for burial. Wang Jisheng, a 23-year-old employee of the Hongxiang Silver Shop on 723 Xinzha Road from Shaoxing, had worked there for eight years and was highly valued by the owner. Recently, Wang suddenly worried that his job might be eliminated, leaving him unemployed and unable to make a living. Overcome with these thoughts, he became disillusioned with life. The day before yesterday, he went alone to the Xinzha Hotel, Room 305, under the alias Wang Jiying, and secretly swallowed potassium cyanide, a poisonous substance, to commit suicide. Around 3 a.m. yesterday morning, he began to suffer from the poison and cried out in pain, which was heard outside the room by the hotel tea boy Huang Rongqing. Seeing that the door was locked, he managed to climb in through the window and, upon seeing the situation, immediately reported it to the Xinzha Police Station, who sent officer Wang Shidong to investigate. An ambulance was summoned, but he died before reaching the Red Cross Hospital. The body was then transferred to the Philan Road mortuary for examination. Around 10 a.m., Tang, a prosecutor from the First Special District Court, arrived to examine the body. According to the police report, Tang confirmed that the deceased, Wang Jisheng, was male and had died from ingesting potassium cyanide. The body was handed over to his mother, Wang Yang, who signed a statement to take it back for burial.

Swarm of Bees Emits White Smoke 126

Fills the Sky Like Clouds and Mist

Scatters on the Ground Like White Sand

Inside the Fifth District Office in Beifuqiao Town, Liuhe Town, Taicang County, there is a ginkgo tree planted during the Ming Dynasty, which is now over 400 years old. The heart of the tree is rotten, and there is a hole near the roots, which has been occupied by bees as a nest for a long time. Recently, on Sunday, several mischievous children poured water into the hole, causing the bees to fly out and hide in a nearby cypress forest. Yesterday morning, the bees suddenly flew around, emitting white smoke from their tails, filling the sky like clouds and mist, and scattering on the ground like white sand. This is recorded to be shared with naturalists.

Dr. Ding Huikang Discusses the Implementation Methods of Tuberculosis Prevention in China 128

National Disease Insurance Endorsed as Key to Successful TB Prevention

Dr. Ding Huikang, director of the Hongqiao Sanatorium in Shanghai, recently gave a lecture on the issue of tuberculosis prevention at the National Shanghai Medical College's commemorative week. He stated that the scope of tuberculosis prevention is extremely broad. Even in countries with advanced medical care, although the mortality rate of tuberculosis has decreased due to advances in medicine, the risk of infection has not diminished. The latest German tuberculosis prevention regulations have not yet been promulgated, and Norway's compulsory hospitalization of patients for treatment, which addresses the root cause, is highly commendable. Given the current complex situation in China, the progress of tuberculosis prevention is not only viewed with indifference by the general public, but even those in the medical field feel helpless. However, considering the severity of the situation, it is imperative that the entire nation work together to undertake this arduous task. Below are my personal suggestions for the implementation of tuberculosis prevention: Medical community has an obligation to report.

The medical community should be at the forefront of tuberculosis prevention and should have an obligation to report tuberculosis patients. This way, within a reasonable period, it is not difficult to obtain tuberculosis statistics. In other words, all severely ill patients (i.e., those who pose a risk of infection) can be clearly statistically tracked after reporting is implemented. Implementation of group checks. Tuberculosis is a kind of communicable disease. X-ray group checks should be performed in all public places such as factories, schools, and companies. Those who are sick should be screened out and isolated. In this way, the risk of transmission can be reduced. This should be done in cooperation between public groups and hospitals. Even general residents who consider themselves healthy should have an X-ray examination by a doctor every year. Attention should be paid to those in an environment with a risk of tuberculosis transmission. Implementation of a method to eliminate the root cause of tuberculosis. All patients with open tuberculosis should be required to be hospitalized for treatment. Their homes should be disinfected. Addressing the root cause is paramount. The authorities should first investigate the number of hospital beds in the city. In the current situation in China, the construction of sanatoriums is also an urgent task. However, whether the architecture should adopt a ward system, a village system, or a mixed system is still a question. Improvement of treatment methods. Currently, natural therapy and condensation surgery are the two most important treatment methods. More importantly, early diagnosis is crucial. Therefore, it is advisable to set up more tuberculosis testing centers in various places, with X-ray and artificial pneumothorax equipment, not only for early diagnosis for the general public, but also for use by private practitioners in the city. Research on tuberculosis drugs. At present, no tuberculosis drugs have been invented in various countries, while China alone has many of them. At the same time, there are many tuberculosis patients in China. What is the crux of the problem? I feel that there is a need for research. Generally speaking, people prefer the convenience of taking medicine rather than the trouble of seeing a doctor. However, if they only see a doctor after the medicine is ineffective, not only do they miss their personal proper treatment period, but the degree of risk of transmission will also increase several times invisibly. This is a serious problem in tuberculosis prevention. Improvement of public health. This is a very broad issue that should be studied by experts. However, in terms of China's social situation, banning spitting is the most important thing. This should be promoted with all efforts. All public institutions and entertainment venues, tickets, and advertisements must have very clear text slogans and pictures, so that everyone is shocked and no longer spits. After one or two years, it may be possible to achieve the goal, and its effectiveness can at least reduce the risk of infection, which is important in tuberculosis prevention. Attention to eugenics. This issue should also be studied by experts. Whether tuberculosis has hereditary properties is still being studied. For example, the Koch Institute in Berlin is raising 3,400 mice to study this hereditary issue. For now, let's not discuss it. However, in terms of the marriage of tuberculosis patients, it not only has a great impact on their personal health, but also has a very high risk of transmission to the other party and their children. This is an inevitable fact. Therefore, from the perspective of tuberculosis prevention, before marriage, both parties should ask a doctor to check the health of their lungs, and then the authorities can issue a marriage certificate. Tuberculosis Museum. It is undeniable that there are many illiterate people in China. In addition, the public's knowledge is shallow. It is difficult to achieve results with text propaganda alone. A tuberculosis museum should be established. The causes of tuberculosis, the routes of transmission, pathological changes, X-ray changes, treatment methods, attention to daily life, and various statistics should all be displayed with pictures and specimens so that viewers can understand at a glance and deeply know the risk of infection and proper treatment methods. The effect will be considerable. Organization of disease insurance. The soundness of this organization is directly proportional to the degree of development of a country's medicine. In China, most patients cannot afford to see a doctor, doctors do not have a fixed income, and their lives cannot be guaranteed. Hospital income is too low and must rely on public and charitable subsidies. Specialized research institutes and complete graduate schools are even unable to develop. Therefore, it is difficult to make progress. Medicine is a noble and positive construction undertaking. Even with national financial resources, it is difficult to maintain. Therefore, this undertaking should be organized by the people of the whole country, the government, and specialized insurance institutions through close cooperation, so that the people have medical security, doctors have a reasonable income, and hospitals have reliable recurring expenses. Then all medical construction can be actively developed. As for tuberculosis prevention, if the disease insurance organization can be fully popularized, the people will have the ability to have early diagnosis and proper treatment, and specialized sanatoriums and research institutes can be established accordingly. Not only can the development of medicine be expected, but the difficult problems of tuberculosis prevention can also be more than half resolved. The above sections may seem unremarkable, but in practice, their implementation not only requires huge economic support, but also considerable time and effort from specialized personnel. A strong and effective organization must be established between social people, private practitioners, university hospitals, and health agencies, and then macroscopic effects can be achieved. This is what we hope for from the joint efforts of our comrades.

Silk and Satin Industry in Hangzhou and Shengze jointly request rectification of industry regulations 130

Trade Association issues open letter to all sectors

Xin Sheng News Agency reports: Recently, competition among retail silk and satin merchants has intensified. The Shanghai Silk and Satin Trade Association previously issued earnest warnings to the Hangzhou Silk Group and the Shengze Silk Group of the association. Because one or two silk and satin stores were selling real silk spun satin at 5.1 fen per foot to attract customers, various customer groups seized on this as an excuse, and rumors spread overseas, raising doubts about the quality and cost of spun satin. Hangzhou, Shaoxing, and Shengze have always been regions producing real silk spun satin, and there is deep concern about impacting sales and endangering the livelihoods of ordinary people. Therefore, they jointly sent a letter to the Silk and Satin Trade Association, requesting correction in accordance with the association's general principles, and requesting a meeting to be convened to effectively rectify industry regulations. The Silk and Satin Association also issued an open letter to all sectors yesterday. The details are as follows:

Open Letter to All Sectors Silk and Satin Trade Association's Announcement to All Sectors: Silk and satin are unique products of our country with a long history, sold both domestically and abroad, used as attire, and welcomed for their durability and beauty. Silk and satin are the result of much human effort and labor; as the saying goes, "every thread is hard-won." From this, it can be understood that although commodity prices have fallen in recent years, there is no reason for silk and satin to be sold at a few fen per foot. Normally, the cost of silk production does not differ greatly; therefore, the selling price of silk and satin should not vary too much. The silk and satin business focuses on small profits and quick turnover. Even when selling at cost, the price should be between 80% and 90% of the original price. Anything beyond this limit is deception, or just old silk and rotten silk. In the past, silk and satin merchants competed by carefully researching ways to improve products and reduce costs by saving expenses. Now, a few retail silk merchants abandon the fundamentals and pursue the superficial, going against the right path. When purchasing goods, they only seek low prices, regardless of quality, in order to make it easier to sell quickly. When selling, they rely on extensive advertising to attract customers, disregarding the increasing business expenses. According to the Dou Shi market, a silk and satin store's daily business is only two or three thousand yuan, but the daily advertising expenses often account for hundreds of yuan. These extra losses must inevitably be borne by the customers. Given this, who can still believe that there are cheap deals for customers? This association, in order to save the reputation of national silk and maintain commercial ethics, believes that it is necessary to correct and put these business malpractices of the industry on the right track. In addition to earnest advice, we must carefully select goods and reduce operating costs to meet the needs of all sectors with affordable and high-quality products. It is well known that what customers want is "genuine goods at fair prices," not just being swayed by deceptive advertising. Now, at the expense of repetition, we hereby formally announce the following, hoping for public understanding: 1. Since ancient times, cheap prices rarely mean good quality. Silk and satin prices have their own reasonable standards. If someone uses unusually low prices to sensationalize, or even uses sacrifices and giveaways to attract attention, their purpose is to lure customers and profit from them. There are definitely no cheap goods. 2. The more intense the advertising, the higher the operating costs, and it can be concluded that there are no cheap goods. 3. All those who advertise "buy one foot, get one foot free" or "buy one, get several free" must have raised the price of the foot of silk itself and have no good goods. 4. All those who limit the time to sell one or two so-called cheap goods for a limited time are not only difficult to buy but also risk being squeezed and injured, resulting in a greater loss than gain. 5. All those who use gifts to please customers should know that the gifts have already been secretly added to the price of the goods, which is no different from paying to buy the gifts. 6. All those who advertise closing sales or clearance auctions often replenish stock as they sell, which is actually a disguised form of opening a store. There are neither good goods nor cheap prices, so please do not be deceived.

Letter from the Two Groups: To whom it may concern, our country's silk and satin business has always valued genuine goods at fair prices, and honesty with all, young and old. In recent times, retail stores, under the guise of commercial warfare, engage in acts of mutual sabotage. Banners of massive discounts are displayed throughout the city. Sacrificing and giving away feet, and buying one and getting several free, are advertised through newspapers and radio broadcasts. Creativity knows no bounds, and every extreme is used. Sometimes, one or two new products or out-of-season goods are marked at attractive prices to lure customers. Customers, unaware, flock to them like ducks. Once the cunning plan succeeds, the deception intensifies. When purchasing goods, they only seek cheap prices, regardless of quality. On the one hand, they deceive customers with inferior goods, gradually causing them to hate domestic silk and admire foreign goods. On the other hand, they prompt silk factories to cut corners and produce shoddy goods in order to meet the selling price. Observing the retail silk merchants in recent years, they only seek discounted goods to meet the needs of the so-called "great sacrifices and great auctions," resulting in low-grade fabrics dominating the market, while fine silk and satin are ignored. If this continues, who will be willing to engage in improving products? As the bad trend spreads, commercial ethics will be completely destroyed, and the reputation of national silk, which has lasted for thousands of years, will also be ruined in one fell swoop. It is already painful to speak of. Unexpectedly, it has recently become even more intensified, with real silk spun satin being sold at one foot or two feet for one fen. Huge advertisements are published in various newspapers, and special programs are broadcast on the radio, with clever and flattering words to sensationalize. It has been investigated that real silk spun satin has always been produced in Shaoxing and Shengze, with a long history and wide sales, reaching all corners of the world. The various territories in Southeast Asia are the main sales destinations. Because it is woven by hand with real silk, the quality is strong and durable, and the profit is extremely thin. Now, one or two retail merchants are using a small number of low-grade goods as a tool to attract customers, labeling them at 5.1 fen, causing various customer groups to seize on this as an excuse, and rumors are spread erroneously in overseas markets, causing doubts about the quality and cost of our country's spun satin, and even suspending procurement, which greatly impacts the national economy and people's livelihood. I recall that the "Diao Chan Crepe" produced by Lie Feng Silk Factory was used as a shouting item by a retail merchant and the price dropped again and again. The major dealers returned the goods, resulting in great losses to the factory. Even now, I still feel cold. However, these one or two Dou Shi merchants are intensifying their efforts, and recently, they have turned their attention to real silk spun satin, sparing no effort to destroy the hundreds of millions of rural workers in Jiangsu and Zhejiang who depend on the family industry for their lives. They are determined to completely cut off the overseas sales of national silk, which is about to be cut off. Thinking of the future, pain and anger mix together. Therefore, we specially request your association to quickly take effective corrective actions in accordance with the association's general guidelines. At the same time, we also pray to convene a meeting to rectify industry regulations, and to formulate strict sanctions against those who destroy the association's goals and engage in actions that are close to destroying national silk, so as to save the decline and maintain national products. We await your urgent command.

However, it was investigated that Feng Yongyuan, Liu Shichang, etc., were all licensed persons who had obtained licenses from the Public Bureau, and were also members of the association. However, the members have died over the years, and their family members have inherited their names without changing them, which is a normal occurrence and cannot be considered illegal. It was resolved that: 1. When the court summons them for trial, all members should appear in court and testify truthfully. 2. The proposal to oppose the rent reduction at the rickshaw owner's meeting on the 27th was passed. 3. The proposal to prepare and issue a manifesto at the general meeting was passed.

Municipal Health Bureau Completes Registration of Private Toilets in Urban Areas 136

Permission to establish 17 toilets

Those not needed are all banned.

The Municipal Health Bureau, in order to pay attention to public health, conducted registration of private toilets in urban areas. Permission to establish private toilets was granted only where it was necessary. Now the registration procedures for private toilets have been completed. There are currently 60 private toilets in urban areas. The Health Bureau believes that only 17 of them are necessary. All unnecessary private toilets have been banned to emphasize hygiene. The private toilets that are allowed to be established will be temporarily used as public toilets and must pay attention to hygiene, such as connecting to sewers and installing tap water, etc., and must pay taxes to the Municipal Finance Bureau. Those who do not follow these procedures will also be banned at any time.

Chinese Medicine and Other Groups Preparing National Medicine Exhibition 140

To be held at the Chinese Medical College starting April 1st

The Shanghai Chinese medicine community, in order to improve domestic medicines, promote planting, and make people aware of medicines, initiated the Shanghai Pharmaceutical Exhibition, jointly with the Shanghai Chinese Medical Association, the Chinese Medicinal Materials Trade Association, the Chinese Pharmaceutical Trade Association, the Ginseng and Bird's Nest Trade Association, and the Municipal Botanical Garden. The preparations have been underway for more than a month, and the work is very intense. The opening exhibition is scheduled to be held at the Chinese Medical College, established by the Chinese Medical Association at the intersection of Henan Road and Bazilu Road, at 2:00 p.m. on April 1st. The details are as follows:

Preparation Status

The exhibition preparation committee has 13 members, nominated by various groups: Qin Bowei, Zhang Zanchen, Chen Cunren from the Shanghai Chinese Medical Association; Dong Bowei, Chen Wenming, Fei Tinghua from the Medicinal Materials Trade Association; Cen Zhiliang, Shen Hefu, Gao Zhiwen from the Chinese Pharmaceutical Trade Association; Yao Changqing, Cui Qifeng, Jiang Rulin from the Ginseng and Bird's Nest Trade Association; and Jiang Ximeng from the Municipal Botanical Garden. The preparation committee has been organized and has held four preparatory meetings at the Medicinal Materials Trade Association to discuss all ongoing matters.

Divisions of Work

The exhibition is organized into four divisions: 1. General Affairs Division, undertaken by the Botanical Garden; 2. Collection Division; 3. Review Division, undertaken by the Medicinal Materials Trade Association, the Chinese Pharmaceutical Trade Association, and the Ginseng and Bird's Nest Trade Association; 4. Publicity Division, undertaken by the Chinese Medical Association. The preparation funds are also shared by the five groups.

Exhibition Contents

The exhibits are divided into three major parts: animal, plant, and mineral. All authentic medicinal materials and valuable treasures are collected and available. Each medicine is marked with its properties, origin, function, producer, etc., and displayed according to decisions. It is clear at a glance for observation and identification. It is truly an unprecedented creation in the Chinese medicine community.

Exhibition Dates

The exhibition is scheduled to be held from April 1st to 30th, divided into three phases: (A) April 1st to 10th, at the Chinese Medical College, established by the Chinese Medical Association at the intersection of Henan Road and Bazilu Road; (B) April 11th to 20th, at the Municipal Botanical Garden at the intersection of Longhua Road and Xinqiaolu Road; (C) April 21st to 30th, at the Medicinal Materials Trade Market in Doutan Lane, Xiangua Street, Nanshi.

Publishing a Special Issue

The special issue of the exhibition will be edited by the Chinese Medical Association. In addition to articles written by various groups, there will be works by well-known medical figures Xie Liheng, Zhang Zanchen, Jiang Wenfang, Ye Jinqiu, Yang Zhiyi, and Zhu Shoupeng. They have unique insights on the exploration and improvement of Chinese medicine. Visiting guests will receive a copy.

One-third higher than the original price

The Communications Bank Handles Agricultural Loans with Success; Over 90% of Loans Granted Last Year Have Been Repaid; This Year, It is Decided to Handle Cotton Planting in Shaanxi and Shanxi, and Tea Planting in Anhui 144

According to the Central News Agency, since expanding its capital, the Communications Bank has dedicated itself to providing agricultural loans. Last year's credit cooperative loan program in Shaanxi Province was very successful. This year, in response to requests from Qimen tea farmers, it will also handle special production and sales loans. The loan situation is explored and recorded as follows:

Cotton Planting Loans in Shaanxi Province: The bank's agricultural cooperative loans are based on cooperatives, mutual aid societies, cooperative preparatory societies, and agricultural warehouses as loan-granting institutions. Last year, loans were first handled in five counties in Shaanxi Province: Dali, Chaoyi, Wugong, Xingping, and Xianyang. Because there was a lack of formal cooperative organizations in the area, credit cooperative preparatory societies were targeted. A total of 80,000 yuan was loaned, which was due in February of this year. Over 90% has been repaid, which is a very good result. The interest rate is a uniform monthly rate of 8%, which greatly benefits farmers. There are now more than 500 formally established cooperatives in these counties. This year, it is decided to loan 200,000 yuan for cotton planting production and sales in Shaanxi Province and, after consultation with the Shanxi Province Cotton Planting Guidance Institute, to simultaneously handle cotton planting loans of 200,000 yuan in Shanxi Province, centered on Yuncheng, including four counties in the area.

Qimen Tea Loans: To promote the recovery of tea trade and improve the economic situation of tea farmers, the bank will conduct short-term tea production and sales cooperative loans in Qimen this year on a trial basis. It is limited to well-organized cooperatives under the guidance of the Qimen Tea Improvement Institute, jointly organized by the Anhui Provincial Government, the National Economic Commission, and the Ministry of Industry. The total amount is set at 500,000 yuan, and the interest rate is a monthly rate of 8%. An office has now been established in Qimen, and tea merchants have also requested loans from the bank for relief, which is currently under discussion. The total amount is 1.1 million yuan, and the loan method will be handled according to ordinary commercial loans.

Now that Wang's residence has been sealed, the public is extremely indignant, so it is decided to continue to request relief from the government.

The Public Security and Health Bureaus are Planning to Establish a Temporary Drug Rehabilitation Hospital 148

Negotiating to Borrow Memorial Buildings in Gaojingmiao for Use; Compiling Regular and Start-up Expenses and Submitting for Appropriation

The Public Security and Health Bureaus of this city, in order to forcibly rehabilitate drug users in the city, have now reached the second phase of registration, and the number of arrested drug offenders is increasing daily. All the existing drug rehabilitation hospitals are unable to accommodate them. With the approval of the municipal government, the two bureaus are jointly planning to establish a temporary drug rehabilitation hospital that can accommodate 500 people. The details are as follows:

Negotiating to Borrow Buildings for Renovation and Preparation

There are more than 4,000 drug users in this city who have voluntarily requested drug rehabilitation from the Public Security Bureau. In addition to the more than 1,730 who have already been sent for rehabilitation, there are more than 2,000 waiting to be sent for treatment. In addition to the 50 beds already added by the Municipal Health Bureau at the Shanghai North Drug Rehabilitation Hospital with existing funds, it is also planned to establish a temporary drug rehabilitation hospital with 500 beds to meet urgent needs. However, it is difficult to find suitable buildings for a hospital with 500 beds in a short period of time. After joint discussion by the Public Security and Health Bureaus, only the memorial village buildings in Gaojingmiao in this city can be renovated and used. According to preliminary estimates, the renovation project will require 5,830 yuan, and the water and electricity connection fees will be 3,300 yuan. However, the memorial village buildings are the property of the Shanghai Local Association, and it is planned to borrow them for a short period of time. It is necessary to first discuss with the Local Association and consult with the Municipal Social Affairs Bureau to temporarily transfer and borrow a portion of the buildings that had been borrowed from the association. Once the hospital is closed, they will be returned. The duration of the temporary hospital is estimated to be three to four months, according to the number of drug users registered with the Public Security Bureau, before it can be completely closed.

Operating Expenses: Minimizing Costs;

In order to save expenses for the establishment of the temporary drug rehabilitation hospital, the necessary funds are used for the application. Therefore, the purchase cost is only over 20,000 yuan. Also, medical equipment and supplies will be transferred as much as possible. The total start-up cost is only slightly more than 21,000 yuan, which is sufficient. However, the location is remote, and security must be taken seriously. A squad of police officers can be allocated by the Public Security Bureau to be stationed there permanently to ensure safety. It is also planned to urge those undergoing rehabilitation to engage in light gardening work to exercise and benefit their physical and mental health. Therefore, the total estimated monthly operating expenses are slightly more than 11,400 yuan. The required expenses have been compiled into a detailed budget by the two bureaus and submitted to the municipal government for appropriation in order to complete the preparations within the month and facilitate drug rehabilitation.

They happened to see the two women shopping on the way and immediately used violent means to force them into the car, intending to take them back to the brothel to resume their old profession. Unexpectedly, while passing the intersection of Haining Road and North Zhejiang Road, the two women took the opportunity to jump out of the car and ran away. Jin Guohua also got out of the car and chased after them. At this time, Hua police officer number 2688 happened to see this and brought the two women and Jin into the police station. After questioning by the police chief, he learned the details. He ordered the two women to be sent to the Jiliang Institute for temporary custody and Jin to be detained. Yesterday morning, he was sent to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special Court. Police lawyer Zhang Tianyin stated the above situation, saying that the incident occurred in Jiangwan. For convenience, he requested that the case be transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for trial. Judge Wu Zehan briefly questioned Chen, Bao, and Jin Guohua, ordering Jin to be detained pending transfer to the Shanghai Local Court Prosecutor's Office, and Chen Cuihong and Bao Guihong to be transferred together.

A straw hut with no number on Route Robert in Shanghai West, Yinhua Lane, caught fire yesterday at 2:48 PM. Central Bank Inspection Report 151

The 275th inspection report on the issuance reserves of Central Bank exchange notes states that, in accordance with the provisions of Article 13 of the Central Bank Law, the council is responsible for inspecting the number of exchange notes issued by the bank and the reserve funds. The 275th inspection was held at the Issuance Bureau of the bank on March 21st, Republic of China's 25th year. The results of the inspection are reported as follows: (A) The total amount of exchange notes issued is 24,865,3401 yuan in silver dollars, including 22,533,516 yuan in silver dollar notes and 2,331,825 yuan in subsidiary currency notes. The total amount of exchange note reserves is 24,865,3401 yuan, including 16,804,5301 yuan in cash reserves. The cash reserves are 13,642,3773.71 yuan stored in the bank's general and branch treasuries and various branches and 3,162,1527.29 yuan stored with peers. The guarantee reserve is 8,060,08100 yuan converted into silver dollars. (B) The total amount of customs gold exchange notes issued is 373,324.7 yuan. The total amount of customs gold exchange note reserves is 373,324.7 yuan. The reserves include 7,351 taels, 9 maces, and 5 fens of gold, which is equivalent to 373,324.7 yuan of customs gold at the fixed price of 5.0779. According to Article 22 of the Central Bank Law, the cash reserve must be at least 60%, and the remainder must be a legal guarantee product as a guarantee reserve. This inspection result shows that the cash reserve exceeds 60%, and the guarantee reserve is within 40%, which is in compliance with the law. This is reported accordingly. March 23rd, Republic of China's 25th year, Chairman of the Supervisory Committee of the Central Bank, Li Xun, Supervisors Xie Mengjun, Yuan Songsun, Qin Qing, Yu Qiaqing, Lin Kanghou, and Xu Jiyin.

Guangdong-Guangxi Industrial Survey Group Report (6) From Wuzhou National Goods Communication

After we arrived in Wuzhou, we immediately toured the city streets. The displays in the shops were indeed mostly national goods, all transported from Guangdong. There were some foreign goods, but only a few. We spoke with Mr. Ma Junwu, the president of Guangxi University. Mr. Ma said that promoting national goods is an essential plan to save the country. The province's self-sufficiency policy is not about Guangxi people using Guangxi goods, but about Guangxi people using national goods from all over the country. In fact, for all businesses run by Chinese people, with Chinese capital, Chinese raw materials, and Chinese workers, their products are naturally popular with everyone. We Guangxi people dare not boast about anything else, but our habit of using national goods is innate. When I went to Shanghai last month, I saw all the goods I needed in terms of materials, and I was very happy. In the future, I can shop without having to seek outside help. Guangxi University has 800 students and is willing to follow you in promoting and advocating this work to save the declining economy. Even local officials and the people are willing to promote it. Regardless of gender or age, everyone is organizing together to work on using national goods. At that time, Chief Huang of the Finance Department and County Magistrate Cai were present, and they all agreed with Dr. Ma's proposal. During the meeting, the atmosphere for using national goods became very strong. Because of the enthusiasm of the Guangxi people's patriotism, promoting national goods is more joyful than in other provinces. We would very much like to seek an opportunity for cooperation with the industrial and commercial leaders of Guangxi Province. Then the development of Guangxi's industry will be limitless, and the promotion of national goods will be even easier.

Overview of Shanghai Grain Merchant Organizations (No. 19 of Shanghai Industry and Commerce Overview) 158

— Edited by China Credit Bureau

The grain industry in this city has a wide variety of types. It can be broadly divided into manufacturing and sales industries. Among the manufacturing industries, it can be further divided into flour, wheat bran, and oilseed cake industries due to the different types of goods. In the sales industry, in addition to the classification of goods, there are also differences between brokerage firms and retailers. Furthermore, due to the differences in regions, it can be divided into foreign merchants and Chinese merchants, local merchants and guest merchants. Therefore, the organizational structure of grain merchants in Shanghai is also unusually complex, and often cannot be understood by outsiders. Based on the survey, I will briefly describe the three categories of rice industry, flour and bran industry, and miscellaneous grains and oilseed cake industry.

I. Rice Industry and Business Group Organizations 159

1. Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Guild. This guild is formed by the combination of the Douye Cuixiu Hall and the Rice Industry Rengu Hall. The Cuixiu Hall was established over a hundred years ago and is the originator of the grain industry organizational body in this city. Even among all the industry associations in the city, there is none that predates it. The bean industry was most prosperous in the mid-Qing Dynasty. The commonly used "98-regulation yuan" in Shanghai was created by them, so it is also called Dou Gui Yuan. However, in recent years, it has gradually declined, but it still has the right to use its own notes, and its receipts and expenditures circulate in the market. Its credit is still very good to this day. The types of business are soybeans, soybean oil, soybean cake, miscellaneous grains, rice, etc., with oilseed cake as the main product, so it is also called the oilseed cake industry. The source of goods is mostly from Guandong and coastal areas of Shandong. This industry is often related to the rice industry, so it is also called the bean and rice industry. In the past, both industries applied to the Shanghai County for transfer of licensing post-its, belonging to the Amaranth rice industry category among the brokerage types.

The Rice Industry Rengu Hall's association also has a long history, but it is later than Cuixiu Hall. It was differentiated from the bean and rice industry, so since the past until now, both parties have cooperated and proceeded consistently in all matters. The persons in charge of the two industries have always been concurrently held by one person. Formerly called directors, now called chairman, the current chairman is Mr. Gu Xinyi. In the last two or three decades, the business of the rice industry has gradually developed, while the bean industry has shrunk. The reason for this is that the bean industry is limited to the local oilseed cake, while the rice industry includes not only Heshadou rice, guest rice, and foreign rice, but also other fancy miscellaneous grains. Even with just the Heshadou rice category, the annual business is considerable due to the large population and huge consumption volume in Shanghai. The business is different, which leads to this.

After 1929, the bean and rice industry associations merged into one and formed the Shanghai Bean and Rice Industry Guild. The general office is located at the Cuixiu Hall in Yuyuan Garden, and north and south market branch offices are set up at the original Rengu Hall and Zhabei. There are many branch organizations affiliated to the association, which are briefly described as follows:

1. Nanshi Bean and Rice Industry Rice Group Rice Distribution Sub-Association. Originally named Nanshi Rice

Industry Association, it is organized by merchants specializing in rice and grain south of the Sixteen PUs in Shanghai South, commonly known as rice distributors. The association is located in the original Rengu Hall address on Zhonghua Road outside Dadongmen. The current director is Mr. Zhu Zixiang.

2. Beishi Bean and Rice Industry Rice Group Rice Distribution Sub-Association. Originally named Beishi Rice Industry Association, it is organized by merchants specializing in rice and grain north of the Suzhou River in Shanghai North and in various parts of Shanghai West. The north end of Xinzha Bridge is the gathering place for rice shops. At its peak two years ago, there were as many as thirty-six, and they all focused on rice as their main business. Merchants and resellers from various places and producing areas also gathered here. The prosperity of Beishi commerce is due to the association's efforts. However, in the past two years, due to the impact of the war, it has declined slightly. The association is located at the intersection of Guangfu Road and Changan Road in Zhabei. The current director is Mr. Guan Zisheng.

3. Bean and Rice Industry Public Weighing Office. Formerly known as Renhetang Public Weighing Office, it was renamed to its current name after the merger of the bean and rice industries. It is organized by merchants specializing in bagged rice and miscellaneous grains in the rice industry, and some merchants who are not members of the Rice Industry Association also participate. The office provides public scales and issues public sampling receipts. The address is attached to the original site of Rentang.

4. Husi Workers' Union. Organized by the Husi of the rice industry. Husi is a rice measuring worker, and their position is very important. Traders consider it more important than apprentices. Below them are tea servants for use. There are hundreds of people in the city. In the past, they were very scattered and not united. After the rice

weighing fairness movement occurred, they suddenly organized and established it. It has not been a year since its founding. The association is located at No. in Yucheng East Lane, Mazhen Road, Zhabei. The current chairman is Mr. Liu Longxiang.

In addition to the above-mentioned groups, there are many other public welfare groups that are organized independently by the rice industry or jointly by the bean and rice industries: such as schools, guilds, and relief funds. Branch institutions have been established one after another. In recent years, warehouses, hospitals, and docks have also been planned. Except for the rice dock, which was established early, and the warehouse, which was completed in 1934, and Mr. Zhang Shengru, the former manager of Dachang Rice Shop, was elected as the director of the warehouse by the guild, other projects are still pending due to the turbulent situation and funding difficulties.

2. Shanghai Rice Milling Industry Association. This association was officially established on February 21, 1918, at the Rengu Hall of the Rice Industry Association. At that time, it was named Shanghai Machine Rice Milling Association. Membership is not limited by the size of the organization, but only those who operate machine rice milling in Shanghai can join, using the president system. However, it is now renamed the Shanghai Rice Milling Industry Association, and the president system has also been changed to the chairman. The internal organizations are modeled after the Rice Industry Association. Therefore, most of the internal administrators are also rice merchants. The current chairman is Mr. Zhu Zixiang, the owner of Xinchang Rice Mill. The association is located at No. 212, Kulun Road, Zhabei.

There are about fifty rice mills in the city recently. Although the larger ones have joined the association early, many of those not yet joined also want to join. Their business mostly involves rice business and self-milling; only a few specialize in milling rice for customers. In addition, there are special ones with business connections, who specialize in milling Ke Lu rice, etc. Among them, Xinchang has the most capital, with eight rice machines, followed by Zhenxing and Heji, etc. (To be continued)

Shen Bao National Goods Weekly

The Relationship Between Cotton Cloth and the Rural Economy 160

— Xiaoshi

There are three main types of cotton cloth: one is machine-made, one is made with new-style machines, and the third is produced by farmhouses. Machine-made and new-style machine-made cotton cloth use completely machine-spun yarn. Farmhouse products are generally half-machine-spun yarn and half-self-spun yarn. These three types of cotton cloth are all essential clothing materials for people's daily life. If everyone can use domestically produced cotton cloth, the rural economy will flourish. China is an agricultural country, and farming and weaving have always been equally important. The so-called "men farm and women weave" is the principle of farm household production. In the rural areas of the interior, there is still a common custom: when a daughter gets married, regardless of wealth, they must make several pieces of cloth clothing, several cloth quilts, and several bolts of cotton cloth. More is considered better. There is a local saying, "Passed down from grandma to mother to daughter," which is considered a good thing. The importance farmers attach to cotton cloth is evident here.

The Xugong Bridge held a farm household economic survey. The entire area had 720 households, 3,536 people, 1,042 spinning machines, and 481 weaving machines. The annual cotton cloth production was 9,387 bolts, worth 9,387 yuan. A recent survey in the improved area of the Shanghai suburbs showed that the entire area had 944 households, 4,904 people, and 862 weaving women. The annual income from cotton cloth was worth 6,750 yuan. According to these two statistics, weaving is indeed the profession of rural women. Although the price of cloth is low and there is no profit to be made, the women in the village are still tirelessly engaged in spinning and weaving. How should we protect and advocate this to maintain her precarious livelihood?

In the past, when I traveled to Jiangyin, the sound of weaving machines was constant in the streets and alleys. Many old weaving machines were dozens, or even hundreds, of them. Few had one or two, or three or four. In addition to women, there were also a large number of men who were weavers. From this, it can be seen that in the rural areas of the interior, not only do women rely on weaving as a career, but there are also many men who use weaving as a career. In Shanghai's Dongjiadu, there are those who specialize in making old-style shuttles, and their business is very good. Small vendors sell them wholesale to various villages. In the Pudong area, women who use weaving as a sideline still account for eight or nine out of ten. Sanlintang native cloth is very famous at the time. I mention these examples to tell everyone the importance of the position that cotton cloth occupies in the countryside. I hope everyone will love and use domestically produced cotton cloth to maintain rural life.

Recently, a friend from Zhenping specifically purchased foot-powered spinning wheels that use artificial spinning in Pudong, because the foot-powered wheels in Pudong can spin three yarns at the same time, unlike the hand-powered spinning wheels in the Suzhou and Wuxi areas, which can only spin one yarn at a time. This friend said that women in the interior who engage in spinning and weaving can support their own minimum living expenses. It can be seen that it is not only necessary to maintain the current state of rural weaving, but also necessary to vigorously promote it. However, the prosperity or decline of industry depends on the sales situation. If patriotic compatriots in various places pay attention to the rural cotton cloth issue and are happy to use domestically produced cotton cloth, the rural economy will flourish. Therefore, my conclusion is, "Use one more bolt of domestically produced cotton cloth, and you can help the livelihood of one more commoner."

How to Maintain a Trade Surplus 161

— Zhu Weixuan

Since the establishment of customs in my country, there have only been huge trade deficit figures on the books every year, but never a single cent of trade surplus. As a result, even the enthusiastic people who originally shouted loudly to promote national goods often became discouraged and retreated due to the lack of results. As a result, the national goods movement became increasingly scattered, and at the same time, the ridicule that the Chinese people received for their five-minute heat has been more than once.

In recent years, people with foresight in my country have realized the importance of economic salvation, so they have proportionally intensified their efforts to promote national goods. Although women's national goods year and students' national goods year did not have significant results, they did not retreat and did not fall into the old trap of five-minute heat. After all, they were victorious. According to reports, the total import volume of Shanghai's foreign trade in December last year was 36,849,949 yuan, and the total export value was 37,932,566 yuan. The trade surplus was 1,082,617 yuan. This is truly the first time since the establishment of customs. Undoubtedly, this is a page of our honor, a harvest of the efforts of those who are enthusiastic about the country's destiny!

However, a month's trade surplus is difficult to compensate for eleven months' trade deficit. Therefore, our only responsibility now is to make further determination and efforts to ensure that the records of each month are trade surpluses, and that the country is permanently transformed from a trade deficit country to a trade surplus country. That is our final success!

To be honest, Chinese goods now have made amazing progress compared to the past. Therefore, the sudden reversal to trade surplus on the customs books in December, although it is said to be the awakening of people's hearts and a deepening expression of national concept, it is also not because there have been considerable substitutes supplied! Therefore, if we want to maintain the trade surplus figure permanently, on the one hand, we must encourage the people to use national goods, and on the other hand, we must also encourage industry, so that Chinese goods can surpass foreign goods. Then the people will also be happy to use national goods. It is not difficult for my country, which has always been in a trade deficit, to transform into a trade surplus country forever!

Finally, the author believes that the national crisis is extremely serious now. Born in a special environment, my country cannot even talk about using force to relieve the national crisis. Therefore, only promoting national goods does not need to be unreasonably interfered with and hindered by external forces. As long as everyone can implement it, it will surely kill the enemy. Compatriots, this is the only way out for our entire nation at present. Let's all get up and work hard!

Promoting Local Goods and Promoting National Goods 162

— Yingfu

Promoting local goods to cultivate the rural economy is indeed the current practical preparation for saving the country. The meaning is so important.

Modern gentlemen such as Tai Shuangqiu and others have therefore initiated a "Local Goods Year" and set a ten-year plan to mobilize the public to promote it together. According to the estimates of these gentlemen, just promoting hand-spun and hand-woven local cloth in the countryside alone, allowing 300 million farmers to engage in this during the five months of slack farming time, even if they earn two cents a day, the annual income will reach 900 million yuan. This shows the importance of promoting local goods in this extraordinary period.

Promoting local goods and promoting national goods can be said to be the left and right wings of the movement to revive the national economy, moving towards a common goal. However, promoting local goods is more strict and easier to achieve practical results than promoting national goods. The reason is: today's so-called national goods (referring to machine-made foreign-style goods), because they are imitated foreign goods, are difficult to distinguish from imported goods. This creates difficulties in identification. At the same time, from the perspective of raw materials, the so-called national goods often have foreign components mixed in. Local goods have fewer of these drawbacks.

Therefore, I also feel that the sentences pointed out in the declaration of the Local Goods Implementation Committee are worthy of our attention:

"We firmly advocate promoting local goods for self-use in the countryside, and promoting urban residents to purchase local goods. We hope that local goods will come to the city, and we do not hope that national goods will go to the countryside. We hope that entrepreneurs will go to the countryside to develop cooperative rural production, and do not absorb rural money into the city to open factories, causing rural financial exhaustion."

Contribution to My Country's Paper Umbrella Industry 163

— Baoyue

Although the manufacturing method of paper umbrellas in our country is very old, it is still quite practical today. In the past, paper umbrellas were an indispensable rain gear for everyone in our country. Since the import of the foreign product "foreign umbrella," people in general have gradually regarded it as an outdated product because of their preference for foreignization, which has greatly hit the paper umbrella industry.

Among the national products that sell well in Nanyang, paper umbrellas are also one of the major ones. The reason why the natives of Nanyang are happy to use paper umbrellas in our country is certainly not only for economic reasons, and they are also suitable for sunshade and rain protection. As a result, paper umbrellas are still selling well in Nanyang today, and they still feel that they are needed.

Although there have been Japanese-made umbrellas imported into Nanyang in recent years, they are not as durable as paper umbrellas made in our country, so the impact on the sales of paper umbrellas in Nanyang is still slight. However, the modern Nanyang natives are no longer as ignorant as they used to be. Because of the invasion of the tide of world material civilization, their minds are gradually becoming new, their knowledge is gradually increasing, and all industries have made considerable progress. Seeing that paper umbrellas can sell well in the market and are profitable, they have set up their own umbrella-making factories. Naturally, in the future, the sales of paper umbrellas in Nanyang in our country will inevitably suffer a major blow.

The Nanyang Sanbaolong Chinese Chamber of Commerce, the consulates stationed in Hezhou, and the Batavia Chinese Merchants Grocery Association have all sent letters to our country's Ministry of Foreign Affairs, requesting that our country's umbrella-making industry pay attention to the worrying future of sales in Nanyang in order to seek improvement and competition. The paper umbrellas shipped to Nanyang for sale are all produced in Wenzhou. Judging from the recent situation of the export of Wenzhou umbrellas gradually decreasing compared to the past, the future is indeed worrying. Of course, we should try to remedy it before it is severely affected, so that it is not difficult to restore the original market situation. However, most of the umbrella-making workers in our country only know how to stick to the old methods and rarely have the ability to research and improve. Now, for the sake of their future lives, they will naturally be very willing and hope that the outside world will contribute opinions.

I think what umbrella-making workers should pay attention to at least is how to reduce costs and strive for beauty. In addition, in terms of materials, domestically produced cotton paper should be used for manufacturing, because it is more durable than foreign kraft paper. Autumn and winter bamboo should be used for bamboo ribs to avoid the occurrence of wormwood. Raw oil has glutinous properties and is easy to break. Use high-quality tung oil. In terms of manufacturing, the toothed wood attached to the umbrella ribs and the tied yarn should be improved. It should be dried in the shade after brushing the oil. Unfinished paper umbrellas should not be packed in boxes. Regarding these points, I hope that my country's paper umbrella industry will refer to them, which are all practical for the improvement of work.

Contributing Opinions 164

Dear Editor: I have a few suggestions for national goods and daily necessities. Please publish them as follows:

Thermos Bottle: It is now sold in poor rural areas, and users find it convenient, but the long form often makes people afraid that it will fall over and break into pieces on the table. This sentence can express the psychology of ordinary users. It is best to ask the manufacturer to improve it, just "weld a round piece of lead inside the bottom of the bottle shell", then it can be placed securely. As for the problem of water leakage from the bottle mouth, the Enthusiastic brand bottle has been improved, so there is no need to say more.

Celluloid Products: The products of Da Zhonghua are the most famous, but unfortunately, they are mostly children's toys (the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted, how many people buy them?). Also, like the pocket memo pads made of celluloid in Japan, no one simply thinks of imitating them. This kind of pad is only three inches square. You can write words on it with a pencil, and then you can erase it with a rubber to use it forever. You can write down in advance what you want to do at home or before going out. It is also very convenient to take out from your pocket if you have something to write down temporarily. If you engrave "Happy New Year", you can also congratulate the New Year. If you send it to a friend, the recipient can also use it for other purposes. I hope the manufacturers will imitate it, but it is profitable.

Enameled Products: The exquisiteness of domestically produced products in recent years is enough to rival foreign products, and there are many types. Only the pots used for cooking at home have not been made. According to foreign products, there is a kind of enamel pot. It is the same shape as the Chinese iron pot, but because it is double-layered, the outside is enamel, and it will not be burnt after a long time, and it is not afraid of coal fire that easily burns pots and kettles. I hope the manufacturers will manufacture it to save the economic welfare of each family in my country, which has the largest consumption. I wish you peace. Luo Shuyi

New National Goods News of the Week 165

The National Goods Industry and Commerce Trademark Sample Exhibition, organized by the Shanghai Municipal People's Education Center, is scheduled to open on April 1. Yesterday, the Shanghai Municipal National Goods Year Association sent letters to various factories for registration.

Dai Yijian, a technician at the Cotton Chemistry Research Laboratory of the Nantong College of Agriculture, has invented the extraction of gasoline, kerosene, and diesel from cottonseed. It is used in automobiles and machines with excellent efficiency. A small factory has now been set up for refining, and a large factory is in progress.

The National Goods Tour Exhibition, initiated by the Shanghai National Goods Factory, is scheduled to open on the 25th at the Fengxian People's Education Center, and will be held in Zhenjiang two weeks later.

The Shanghai Municipal National Goods Year Association held its sixteenth executive committee meeting on the 22nd and decided to set up a design and economic committee and hire powerful people from the national goods industry as committee members.

The Ningxia Provincial Government solicited products for the provincial national goods exhibition hall and sent a letter to the Shanghai Municipal Government to order the Shanghai national goods group to handle it.

Tianyuan Electrochemical Factory manufactures pure hydrochloric acid, which has recently been produced in large quantities and is sufficient for domestic scientific applications.

The Patriotic Youth Liang Tongfang, Fan Renliang and others organized a national goods promotion group, which has set off yesterday to the Yangtze River area, surrounding cities and rural villages across the country, to conduct on-the-spot propaganda.

The Overseas Chinese Importers Association in the Dutch East Indies sent a letter to the Shanghai National Goods Factory Federation, stating that the Dutch East Indies allows the import of national goods without restrictions, and the population tax is the same as that of other countries, and there are no harsh cases.
