Farewell Commemoration Xu Chengji Battles Carson Today 166

Starting at 3:30 PM at the China Tennis Club Cai Huiquan Left Shanghai Yesterday Morning to Meet in Hong Kong

Mr. Xu Chengji, my country's Davis Cup tennis representative at this session, is scheduled to board the Italian Post Victoria at 11:00 AM tomorrow to leave the country. Before leaving, Mr. Xu originally planned to hold multiple exhibition matches in Shanghai, but due to the cold weather, it has not been held. Now that Mr. Xu's departure date is approaching, in order to thank him for his enthusiasm, he will be with Mr. Carson, a Western tennis master, at the China Tennis Club, No. 5 Singapore Road at 3:30 PM this afternoon. Hold a singles exhibition match. According to Mr. Xu, on the day after arriving in Shanghai, he defeated Carson by three to one. When the two heroes meet again, there will be a more exciting performance. In addition, the newly advanced tennis master Cai Huiquan has decided to accompany Mr. Xu and Mr. Lin Baohua and his wife to France at his own expense. Because he still has private matters to deal with in Hong Kong, he returned to the south by boat yesterday morning and waited for the Victoria to pass through Hong Kong. Then I will meet with Xu Lin and others to go to France together.

Hong Kong First Division Football League South China South Failed Again 167

Lost to the Navy with a score of 1 to 2 Malaysian Zhang Xianyuan Participated in the War

Hong Kong, 24th Electric Dispatch. In the Hong Kong Ordinary Cup, South China South played against the Navy. The South team's points were gradually decreasing, and the hope of winning the championship was shaken. Therefore, it fought with all its strength on this day, and appointed Zhang Xianyuan, a newly returned Overseas Chinese athlete from Malaysia, as the center forward. In the second half, Zhang and Li switched positions, but it was still ineffective. Instead, the Navy scored two goals. As a result, the Navy won 2 to 1.

The Ministry of Education's Edited "Detailed Items for Elementary School Physical Education Teaching": Elementary School Physical Education Teachers Nationwide Rush to Purchase and Read 178

The "Detailed Items for Elementary School Physical Education Teaching," edited by the Ministry of Education, inviting physical education experts Wu Yunrui, Chen Meiying, and Chen Kuisheng, in accordance with the elementary school physical education curriculum standards, has been published by the Shanghai Sima Road No. 27 Bookstore. The book consists of four volumes. The first volume provides a general discussion and explanations of operational requirements, instructing on elementary school physical education teaching methods. The second volume provides demonstrations of various teaching materials. The third volume covers rhythmic activities. The fourth volume covers gymnastics and sports. It contains all the physical education materials for six years of elementary school, such as dances, songs, and song and dance, standard exercises, ordinary exercises, and Tai Chi exercises, track and field, ball games, ground movement, skill movements, and light equipment exercises. The end of the book includes a plan for elementary school physical education equipment, which is a must-have book for elementary school physical education teachers. The entire set of four volumes costs one yuan and forty cents. For mail orders, add sixteen cents for registered postage. Elementary school physical education teachers across the country are rushing to purchase and read the book from Qinfen Bookstore and teach their students according to the teaching materials in the book.

The Ministry of Education Rectifies the Capital's Student Attire and Appearance 180

(Nanjing, 24th) In order to rectify the attire and appearance of students in the capital, the Ministry of Education has formulated five general principles for implementation: 1. Students above the junior college level must wear uniforms immediately. 2. Regarding students' posture, each school should provide practical instruction and should appoint specialists to correct and guide students anytime and anywhere on and off campus. 3. Female students should also wear uniforms uniformly, following the procedures stipulated by the ministry. 4. For secondary school student uniforms, a unified style should be adopted next semester.

French Mathematician Hadamard to Give a Public Lecture at Jiaotong University 185

Visited the Municipal Government in the Morning, Went to Jiaotong University in the Afternoon, and Attended a Public Banquet Hosted by Various Academic Organizations in the City in the Evening. Will Go to Japan in a Few Days and Plans to Return North During the Spring Vacation.

After the arrival of the French mathematical genius Hadamard and his wife in Shanghai, they visited the city center in the morning and gave a public lecture at Jiaotong University in the afternoon at the invitation of the Chinese Science Society and other organizations. Various academic organizations and the Sino-French Friendship Association hosted a banquet in the evening. Details are as follows:

Visiting the Municipal Government: At 9:00 AM yesterday, Hadamard and his wife traveled by car to visit the city center. Secretary-General Yu and Xu Peihuang, Li Dachao, and others guided them in visiting various municipal bureaus and the construction of the stadium and municipal hospital. Hadamard expressed his deep admiration for the various construction projects in the center. They returned to the International Hotel to rest at around 11:00 AM and made ordinary social calls to visitors.

Welcome at Jiaotong University: At 3:00 PM in the afternoon, Mr. and Mrs. Hadamard arrived at Jiaotong University. Accompanied by the deans of the various colleges, they visited for a week before holding a tea party welcome in the Ronghong Hall. More than ten people attended, including Li Peihuan, Zhang Tingjin, Qiu Weiyu, Hu Yifu, Gu Yangwu, Hu Gangfu, and Hu Duanxing, Fan Huiguo, and Zhu Gongjin, Xu Mingcai. During the tea party, Shan Lishao Huan delivered a welcome speech, expressing his respects.

Public Lecture: At 4:30 PM, the Chinese Science Society, the Chinese Mathematical Society, the Chinese Physical Society, and Jiaotong University invited Hadamard to give a public lecture in the Engineering Hall. Five to six hundred people from all walks of life attended. Li Zhaohuan first gave a brief introduction, followed by Hadamard's lecture, entitled "The Relationship between the Theory of Partial Differential Equations and the Theory of Real Variables." Hadamard lectured in fluent English, clarifying the relationship between partial differential equations and function theory with novel and precise arguments. The Chinese Mathematical Society sent a member to the scene to record, and the recorded lecture will be published separately later.

Sino-French Tea Party: At 5:30 PM in the afternoon, the Sino-French Friendship Association, the French Literary Society, and other organizations held a tea party welcome at the French Engineering Department Auditorium at No. 11, Huanlong Road. The Deputy Chairman of the French Literary Society, De Gaotuo, the Chief Representative of the General Assembly in Shanghai, Gao Boai, and all directors and Secretary Lin Jun of the French Literary Society, and the Chairman of the Sino-French Friendship Association, Zhao Zhiyou, were responsible for the reception. Guests included the French Consul General Batteres, the French Consul Bilihong, the Commercial Counselor Sachin, the Director of the French Engineering Department, Wei Zhiren, the Commander of the French Far East Fleet, Commander Aisiling Aiside, the Commander of the French Army, Fei Xubang, the Chief Inspector of the French Concession Police, Fabre, the Deputy Chief Inspector, Pre-and-Post President of Aurora University School Principal Hu Wenyuan and French School President Xue Fan of Sino-French Institute of Technology, National Government French Advisor Badao, and Chu Minyi, Qu Junqian, Jiang Wenxin, Nong Ruhui, and over fifty others, who exchanged greetings. They dispersed at around 6:00 PM.

Public Banquet Hosted by Organizations: At 7:00 PM, the Chinese Science Society, the Chinese Mathematical Society, and the Chinese Physical Society held a joint banquet at the Huaan Building on Jing'an Temple Road, with over a hundred members of the three societies attending. Cai Yuanpei delivered a welcome speech, followed by Hadamard's reply. They parted with joy at around 10:00 PM.

Leaving for Japan in a Few Days: It is reported that Mr. and Mrs. Hadamard do not intend to stay in Shanghai for long. After visiting Hangzhou in two or three days, they must go to Japan for about a spring vacation before returning to Shanghai to lecture in the north. It is also reported that Hadamard has not yet expressed his opinion on his impression of Shanghai during this visit, but he has praised the various construction projects of the municipal government.

City Education Bureau Notice: Elementary School Spring Vacation Extended 188

Children's Day is on April 4th, Changed to Start on April 5th

The Shanghai Municipal Education Bureau issued an order to public and private elementary schools yesterday: According to the instruction No. Pu Si Chang 3398 issued by the Ministry of Education on March 17, 1936, the National Children's Year Implementation Committee stated that the committee previously decided to hold a joint commemoration of Children's Day on April 4th and the elementary school spring vacation from April 1st to April 7th, which caused many inconveniences. The committee requested the Ministry to change the date of the elementary school spring vacation. However, no instructions have been received yet. At the committee's tenth meeting, it was resolved that Children's Day on April 4th of this year, which is Children's Year, is of greater significance than in previous years, and an expanded celebration will be held to commemorate it. However, holding it during the spring vacation would cause many inconveniences in preparation and assembly. The committee should submit a document to the Ministry of Education requesting the postponement of this year's spring vacation to start on April 5th, and notify the education bureaus of all provinces and cities to instruct their affiliated elementary schools to comply. In view of this, considering that April 4th of this year is Children's Day of Children's Year and to facilitate the preparation and assembly for the grand celebration, this year's elementary school spring vacation will be temporarily postponed to start on April 5th, as requested. This order is hereby issued to the schools under your jurisdiction to comply accordingly.

Guangdong Vigorously Implements Mass Education 189

Guangzhou City Promotes Literacy Campaign

Guangning County Increases Short-Term Elementary Schools

Haifeng County Holds Nine People's Schools

Guangzhou Communication: Since the implementation of the three-year plan in Guangdong Province, mass education has been actively promoted. In order to implement the literacy campaign, the Guangzhou City Party Department established a Literacy Campaign Committee to specialize in this matter. The Municipal Education Bureau also established a Mass Education Committee, and the City Party Department also sent personnel to jointly organize it. The city is now divided into six districts, and mass education committees are first established in Henan, Dongguan, and Xiguan. In addition to paying attention to awakening national consciousness, the Mass Education Committee especially emphasizes the literacy campaign. A literacy textbook has been compiled and will be distributed by party members of all levels of the party, various groups, and teachers and staff of municipal schools, who will be responsible for conducting surveys, organizing teaching, and other matters. According to statistics, there are approximately 300,000 illiterate people in the city. It is now planned to organize teaching by region and occupation, in stages and groups, in order to eliminate illiteracy. In order to promote compulsory education, Guangning County opened more than 100 short-term elementary schools last year. This year, it is vigorously promoting this, planning to add 15 short-term elementary schools, selecting impoverished areas in various districts of the county to establish them. The principals have been recruited and are responsible for preparing, and the schools have started classes in February of this year. In order to eliminate illiteracy and reduce the number of out-of-school children in the county, the Haifeng County Education Bureau initiated the establishment of nine people's schools, which have been established at selected locations.

Jiangsu Province Education College Achievement Exhibition 190

The Ninth Achievement Exhibition of Jiangsu Provincial Education College opened on the 14th. The exhibition and performances were held simultaneously. On the morning of the 15th, the college also held an eight-week anniversary celebration. Over the past two days, visiting groups included educational and agricultural institutions such as the Provincial Luoshe Rural Teachers' School and the Provincial Luoshe Rural Teachers' School, and the Provincial Sericulture Experiment Station. Educational and agricultural experts included Zou Shuwen, Dean of the Agricultural College of Central University, Zeng Jikuan, Deputy Director of the Jiangsu Provincial Agricultural Improvement Committee, Li Yunting, President of Beijing Normal University, Liu Jihong, President of Henan University, and Tai Shuangqiu, Dean of the Education College of Great China University. Niu Tiesheng, Vice President of the Examination Yuan, Wu Zhihui, a member of the Central Committee, Wu Jianzhen, Section Chief of the Education Department, Peng Baichuan, Magistrate of Kunshan County, and others attended. It was estimated that several thousand people visited each day. On the afternoon of the 14th, several foreign ladies also visited. They praised the various achievements on display. The walls of the National Crisis Education Exhibition Room were covered with charts of the international situation and lost territories of our country. Xu Gongjian, a teacher at the Education Department of Great China University, has in-depth research on mass education and has written many works. His previous book, "Practical Methods of Mass Education," was published by Datong Bookstore and became popular throughout the country. Those engaged in mass education rushed to buy and read it. Now, he has compiled dozens of papers he has written on mass education over the years into a single collection, entitled "Collection of Essays on Mass Education, Volume 1." The content is rich, totaling 180,000 words. It contains insightful discussions on issues such as the theory, implementation, and practice of mass education. It has now been published by Great China University and is listed as one of the books on mass education. It is sold at the Great China Bookstore on Zhongshan Road in Shanghai, and at the Kaiming Bookstore, Life Bookstore, and Author's Bookstore on Fourth Avenue. The actual price is 80 cents, but there is a special discount of 20%.

Survey of Schools: Overview of Shanghai American School 193

— Hu Zuyin

There are quite a few schools established in Shanghai, especially those established by foreign nationals. In recent years, educators from various parts of the country who come to Shanghai to visit education facilities often want to see the overall facilities of foreign schools, in order to learn from them. However, due to language and time constraints, they often cannot get a complete picture. Now, we are introducing an overview of Shanghai American School as a reference for educators. Overviews of schools established by nationals of other countries in Shanghai will be published successively later. The author would like to thank Dr. Wells, the principal of Shanghai American School, for providing materials and for donating a bird's-eye view of the school building. (Editor's note)

1. The largest American school in China

Shanghai American School is the largest American school in China established by American expatriates for their children. American expatriates from all provinces in China send their children to the school. Most of the students come from American expatriates living in Shanghai, but there are also students from Jiangsu, Guangdong, Fujian, Zhejiang, Hainan, Shandong, Hong Kong, Yunnan, Anhui, Henan, Hubei, Jiangxi, and Manchuria.

The school was established on September 17, 1912. It was initially organized by a group of parents from the staff of three American churches and the YMCA in China. At that time, a board of directors was established in New York to oversee all school affairs. The school's purpose was to educate American children in an American school by American teachers using American ideals and traditional concepts, so as to cultivate them into the most useful American citizens. The school's organization includes a complete elementary school and a two-level secondary school.

The school was quite small when it was founded. It rented a house on North Sichuan Road as a school building. In the first semester, there were only 38 students. In September 1923, the school moved to its current location, 10 Avenue Petain in the French Concession. The new school building has a large site, covering approximately 938 mu. Therefore, the number of students, school buildings, and equipment have all developed greatly over the years. Initially, most of the children enrolled came from church and business families in China. Therefore, an executive department was established in Shanghai in 1921, jointly maintained by an equal number of representatives elected by churches and businesses in China, while a permanent board of directors was established in New York to manage all school affairs. The members of the board of directors and the executive department are all elected from related groups, and are partially re-elected annually.

Bird's-eye view of the Shanghai American School building

Odds and Ends 217

— (Ji Yijie)

There are rarely people who stand on the same front with each other. They are either sleeping in the same bed with different dreams or going their separate ways. In a nutshell, they are driven by selfish desires. Different mentalities form different contradictory facts. So-called unity and so-called cooperation are all nonsense.

Money and power are mutually reinforcing. Having money without power is like a three-legged cow that cannot stand firmly. Having power without money is like a two-legged tiger that cannot jump. Only when money and power are mixed together can things be accomplished and people be harmed.

Someone's lackey, someone's henchman, on the surface, seems loyal to someone. But if that person falls out of favor one day, they will go and follow someone else to live their lackey's and henchman's life. If their new master is your enemy, they may even turn against you and attack you until you are completely battered and bruised. Those who plant parties and pursue private interests can rest.

The world is getting worse day by day, people's hearts are sinister, they deceive each other, and they squeeze each other out. Good people who are currently good will have no place to stand. If you want to be a good person, you must uphold justice and strive to fight against evil people. If you have good intentions and he has bad intentions, the result will still be in vain.

Talking About Azaleas 218

— Shijiu

The myriad colors of spring can certainly delight the eye; however, there are also those who yearn for home and feel melancholy and lament when facing flowers. Among all the flowers, the most likely to evoke thoughts of separation is the azalea. Li Bai, in Xuancheng, upon seeing the azalea, wrote a poem saying:

"I once heard of the cuckoo bird in the Shu Kingdom, and now I see azaleas in Xuancheng. Each cry breaks my heart, and every spring month I remember Sanba."

According to legend, the cuckoo bird is also called the azalea bird. When it cries, its voice is mournful, as if calling "It's better to return home," which is enough to stir the traveler's thoughts of returning home. Moreover, the azalea flowers bloom all over the valleys, and seeing them naturally makes one's heart break.

The azalea is also known as the mountain pomegranate. Bai Juyi's poem to Yuan Jiu says, "Mount Shang and Qin Mountains are frightening, mountain pomegranate flowers are red along the road!" This also means that azalea flowers evoke people's sorrows.

There is also a story that is extremely sad and glamorous. Langhuan Ji says:

"Once, someone was drinking at the Xie family in Jincheng, and the daughter peeked and was pleased by him. When everyone heard the cuckoo singing, they left Xie's house. The daughter hated it very much. Later, when she heard the cuckoo singing, she was startled like a leopard. She ordered the maids to drive it away with bamboo branches, saying, 'Do you still dare to come here and sing!' Therefore, the cuckoo is called Xie Leopard."

Although this story seems unrelated to azalea flowers, the time when azaleas bloom is the time when cuckoos sing sadly. Therefore, azalea flowers are also called Xie Leopard flowers, as seen in Gewu Bian.

In the Tang Dynasty, azalea flowers seemed to be very precious. Wang Jian's Palace Poems says:

"Taiyi came from the warm room the other day, and asked Zhaoyang to beg for medicine to plant; the emperor bestowed a clump of red rhododendrons, and before thanking him, he reported that the flowers had bloomed." According to legend, azalea flowers are also called mountain rhododendrons, as also seen in Gewu Bian.

Matching this poem, there is Bai Juyi's playful question about mountain pomegranate flowers, saying:

"A small mountain pomegranate tree is planted near the steps, half containing red sepals and bringing flowers: How can I know that Sima's wife is jealous, and it will not bloom when moved to the courtyard."

The previous poem says "Before thanking him, he reported that the flowers had bloomed," which is so joyful! This poem says "It will not bloom when moved to the courtyard," which is so sad! Mr. Bai's wife must be a female tiger!

"So Warm" 219

— Hualing

Although he also started as a coolie, he is now "so warm." He is "so warm," the leader of that group of coolies. Although his shoulders used to carry carrying poles, and his legs used to be beaten with rattan sticks, now he doesn't touch the carrying pole with his fingers. In hot weather, he wears a short silk gauze shirt and trousers. In cold weather, he wears a wadded coat made of horse-cloth. With a cigar in his mouth and a rattan whip in his hand, he paces back and forth among a large group of coolies, scolding Zhang San from time to time, or beating Li Si's legs with the rattan whip.

"So warm, there are so many goods recently, and the pieces are so big. Our group of coolies is really a bit overwhelmed. Please do a good deed and ask the foreman to add a few more people to the group," a coolie pleaded one day.

"Bullshit, who says they can't handle it? Whoever says that can get out of here, that's it. If the foreman finds out about this, he will definitely fire all of you. The foreman is still saying that he can't make money this year and is thinking of reducing the number of people in the group," So Warm said with a sneer.

A few days later, someone pleaded again: "So warm, everything is so expensive now. We work twelve hours a day and still don't get six dimes. If we get sick for a day, we have to deduct four dimes. It's really not enough to live on. Please have mercy and give us seven dimes a day according to the number in the guild. So warm, do a good deed, and God will bless your second concubine to give birth to a fat son this year."

"What are you talking about? The guild issues four dimes and eight cents per worker. Who said seven dimes? Whoever said seven dimes can come and be So Warm... Hmph, let me tell you, when the No. 14 pier was being rebuilt, more than 600 coolies came to me to make contact, each paying a deposit of 300 yuan, with a daily wage of five dimes. I thought you were all pitiful, so I didn't agree to them. I think you should be more well-behaved. If the foreman finds out, he will definitely fire all of you. The ringleader will have to sit in a foreign prison. By then, you won't be able to handle it."

Business is booming day by day. Later? The foreman also felt that it was necessary to increase the number of coolies in the group. So he ordered So Warm to increase a group. But So Warm did not recruit new workers. Instead, he increased the working hours of each of the existing day and night shift coolies by six hours and increased their wages by three dimes. But this was So Warm's special grace to the coolies, so they all willingly fulfilled So Warm's condition of extracting half a dime from each person. Because the coolies had the labor, and working six more hours was fine, after all, they had an income of two and a half dimes a day.

But in less than three months, So Warm married a third concubine.

Notes on What I Saw 222

— (Xie Yun)

It was a warm and sunny early spring afternoon. I took a steam train (small train) from Zhenru to Shanghai. The train wheels rumbled on the rails. I leaned against the train window and looked at the houses in the distance. The smoke from the factory chimneys drifted in the air like swimming dragons with the wind. The sky was blue and clear, and the scenery was beautiful. After the train passed Zhongshan Road, when it was approaching the temporary station of the Sun Temple in Zhabei, I saw from afar that there were two black, long packages lying next to the railway sleepers. When the wheels slowly passed, I looked down and saw that they were actually two dead babies. One was a little bigger, and the other seemed to have just been born. Their ochre-red faces were covered with sparse brown hair, lying silently in the packages. I don't know whose illegitimate children they were, or whether they were abandoned here because they were too poor to bury them after death. The wheels continued to move forward, leaving this shocking tragedy behind. At this time, my heart was thumping, echoing the spinning wheels. These two small lives had lost their vitality. This can only be blamed on them for being born in pitiable China, where society is powerless to raise them, so they are abandoned like spittle. Seeing so many strong and lively young people sacrificing themselves to hunger and bandits, I don't know how many there are, let alone these little lives with their milk hair not yet dry and unable to resist all attacks? If they were born in a strong country, they would be in a nursery being raised at this time. How could they have died without anyone to bury them?

Little Common Sense

How Food Transforms Into Flesh and Blood 223

— Hu Chuyu

We eat food every day to sustain life and avoid starvation. But what actually happens inside our bodies after we eat? How does digestion occur, and how do the nutrients absorbed through digestion transform into flesh, blood, muscles, and bones? We should understand this basic knowledge. Generally, after food enters our bodies, it changes its original shape and nature within a few hours. A portion of it becomes various substances within the body. The subtle changes rely on the power of "acid enzymes" to function. Now, I will briefly explain the process of these changes.

Each time we eat, the food enters the stomach. The gastric juice contains an enzyme called "Pepsin." With the help of hydrochloric acid, it initially acts on the proteins in the food, transforming them into "Peptone." This involves breaking down the proteins into "Amino acids." Then, in the intestines, the pancreatic juice secreted by the pancreas contains the enzyme "Trypsin." With this enzyme, the proteins are more easily digested. Also in the pancreatic juice, the enzyme "Amylase" acts to transform starch, which is then absorbed as sugars. Simultaneously, the enzyme "Lipase," along with bile from the gallbladder, manages the digestion of fats very effectively. In the intestinal fluid within the intestines, the enzyme "Erepsin" acts due to the effects of "Pepsin" and "Trypsin," breaking down the digested proteins more thoroughly into amino acids. Thus, our digestive organs perform highly specialized digestive functions. The nutrients digested and absorbed in this way are distributed to various parts of the body by the blood. Upon reaching various tissues, they combine with enzymes already present. Glucose becomes "Glycogen" (a colorless, odorless, tasteless, and non-crystalline substance present in the muscles and liver of the human body, which decreases when we are hungry or tired). Amino acids transform into muscles. Dissolved in water combined with other organic substances, the enzyme "Phosphatase" on the surface of bones breaks down to form "Calcium phosphate," transforming into bone. When we work, we need energy (Energie). How is this energy produced? It is because of the burning of "Glycogen" in the muscles (the term "burning" does not mean like burning charcoal with fire and high temperature, but rather burning at the body temperature of about 37 degrees Celsius). First, glycogen is converted into glucose through the action of enzymes, and then oxidation enzymes cause the burning process. However, ordinary glucose is a white crystalline substance that requires a heat of over 200 degrees Celsius to burn. Why does it burn at a body temperature of only 37 degrees Celsius? This is due to the action of the incredible enzymes. On a daily basis, our movements (such as the movement of limbs) require the work of oxidation enzymes. The heart muscle works tirelessly day and night because of the presence of strong oxidation enzymes. As for enzymes, they lose their effectiveness at temperatures above 80 degrees Celsius. Furthermore, from the perspective of plant growth, seeds that are as hard as stone can sprout and grow into towering trees when exposed to suitable temperature and moisture. This incredible phenomenon is also due to the action of enzymes, which create the stems, leaves, and branches.

Shanghai News Supplement

Talks

Arson Burning of Shantytown Incident 235

— Mengruo

The shantytown on Yutong Road in Zhabei has recently been repeatedly forced to relocate by landlords, and we are speaking out for the hundreds of poor people there. Unexpectedly, on the morning of the 7th, the thatched huts there were twice set on fire by arsonists, which is even more unfortunate for them. Although this disaster did not escalate into a major calamity, the incident itself cannot be ignored.

First of all, we must talk about the forced relocation. The open space there was leased to a landlord. Now, because the landlord wants to build houses, he is forcing the residents to relocate. However, the shantytown residents are all refugees from various places. Once their houses are demolished, they will have nowhere to live. Therefore, once the landlord evicts them, they are all in a state of panic. So they jointly submitted a petition to the party and government authorities, begging for help and appealing to the landlord to postpone the forced relocation. From the landlord's point of view, the open space belongs to him, leasing it was his act of kindness, and reclaiming it is his right. Therefore, forcing them to relocate is a legitimate matter. But from the shantytown residents' point of view, they are all poor people. They can only afford to live in thatched huts and have no money to rent houses. Once they are forced to relocate, where will they live? Therefore, their request to postpone the forced relocation is a last resort. Now that the landlord is repeatedly urging them, he is not considering the plight of the poor.

Secondly, we must mention the arson incident. Who committed the arson is unknown before the truth is revealed. But although we dare not determine who the criminal is or who instigated him, it is undoubtedly related to the forced relocation. There are several pieces of evidence. The arson occurred after the land was reclaimed. There would be no reason to commit arson for no reason. The shantytown residents also pointed out several suspects in their petition. If our guess is correct, then the seriousness of this matter is very obvious.

Regarding the handling of this incident, we have three suggestions. The first is to severely punish the perpetrators. Deliberately setting fire to houses is a criminal offense. Fortunately, the fire was extinguished early, so only a dozen thatched huts were burned. If the fire had been allowed to spread, the consequences would have been unimaginable. Not only would all the thatched huts have been burned down, but the lives of hundreds of residents would have been in danger of being burned to death. Therefore, the authorities should strictly pursue the perpetrators and investigate the instigators behind the scenes, and punish them according to the law. The second is that although the landlord's forced relocation of the shantytown residents is reasonable, he should allow a longer period of time for each resident to find a place to live. This is of great importance to the lives of the poor. Therefore, the landlord should not force them too much, and the authorities should mediate the matter. The third is that we hope that the authorities will understand the difficulties of the people and make arrangements for the residents to resettle and provide relief.

Patrol Officer 236

— Dongguang

Leaving Lao Nangua's gambling den, it was still drizzling outside. Spring evenings turn dark in the blink of an eye. The streets were deserted, the roads were full of puddles and mud, and the shops on both sides were lit with large Mobil lamps. The shop assistants were slumped on the counters, silently watching the misty rain scene in the center of the street.

The rain fell softly, and the tiny drops of water, when blown onto my feverish face, brought a cool and refreshing sensation. Liu Yuchang moved his short, fat body, walking ahead of me. He was wearing the newly issued yellow military uniform, with his hat tilted on his forehead, swaying like a drunkard. He was singing "Widow Yearning for Spring" in his hoarse voice. After singing for a while, I followed him silently. When we were almost at the edge of the village, he suddenly turned his face and asked:

"Patrol Officer, how was your luck today?"

"Lost more than three dollars."

The two of us fell silent again. I knew he was very happy today. He had only been in the gambling den for half an hour and had won two reds in a row, so he stopped playing. He bought half a dollar's worth of opium paste from Lao Nangua and smoked a lot of it, and said he would go to the Da Jin surgical clinic at night. As for me, it was worse than touching a nun's breasts and putting them back in the treasure box - four blacks. Good, another three dollars disappeared. At this time, we walked out of the village. There was a slope, and Liu Pangzi slipped and fell. When he got up, he had rolled into a mud lion. Muttering to himself, he walked to the entrance of the station. Without saying a word to me, he turned around and went inside to change his clothes. I grabbed his arm, and he jumped down from the steps and looked at me with surprised eyes, saying:

"What?"

"The Director told me to get there, what is it?! Is he even in charge of marrying wives and raising sons?!"

I glared at him. He ignored me and ran inside. I calculated in my mind that I was out of luck because of this bastard. If he hadn't asked me to go, I might have won back my money and then won a few more dollars from him. Thinking this, I walked into the backyard. Listening to the Director's room, it was very quiet. I pulled open the door of the outer room, and the Director coughed a couple of times and asked:

"Who is it?"

I quickly replied, and hurried into the inner room.

The Director was lying on the bed alone, smoking opium. He raised his head, squinted at me in the light, and said:

"Why are you back so late?"

I didn't dare to say anything, standing at the door with a red face. After a while, I stole a glance at the Director and saw that he didn't look like he was going to scold me, so I felt a little relieved. He kept his mouth tightly closed, looked at the teacup, and I quickly picked up the teapot, poured a cup of tea and handed it over. He swallowed it in one gulp, and then slowly let a wisp of gray smoke filter out of his mouth. Sitting up straight, he lit another cigarette and slowly instructed:

"Yes, yes."

I slipped out quietly.

The brothers were arguing in the room about the case of catching the adulterer the day before. I passed through the small moon gate and was about to yell at them when suddenly one of the brothers in the room said:

"What did the Director tell the Patrol Officer to do again?"

"That kid Wu Zhan Kui will only add屁骨(a person who sucks up to someone) for the Director and make good deals!"

As soon as he finished speaking, everyone laughed. I was so angry that I really wanted to rush in and hit them, but thinking about it, I decided to endure it. I stood in the rain for a while, pretending to be coming back from outside. Coughing, I opened the door and forced a yawn as I walked into the room.

Green Willow River 237

— Rice Mountain

Green Willow River roars angrily every day, like a tiger being chased, wearing clothes of yellow sand woven into waves, running from our village to the Shandong border.

I'm afraid it has been angry like this since it had this river. According to the noble gods, it manages all the mountains and rivers in the world. Green Willow River naturally belongs to its management. However, Green Willow River is sometimes very naughty, causing the gods to be angry, punishing it to run for life until it dries up.

However, we have a saying that goes, "When the cypress tree sheds its leaves, the stone roller (agricultural tool for flattening ground) flows with its heart, and the Green Willow River dries up on the shore, the world will be peaceful." This tells us that Green Willow River will not dry up. Our place will never have peaceful days.

No one understands why our days are getting harder and harder. Grandfather often shook his head sadly, twirling his beard and saying, "In the past, every family was happy. Thanks to the gods' blessing, we were the gods' happy people, but...but since the foreigners came..."

In my memory, there has never been happiness.

We live in a village of twenty-nine families, close to the river bank, looking out at the glittering desert, our houses built low on the sand by the river bank. Six or seven people live together in the whole family.

In the morning, we dry the fishing net and prepare for the day's work. That work is very hard, often busy all day, and we don't get much. Although our shoulders and backs are as tired as if they have fallen apart.

The old people tell us: In the past, there was never such a hard life. At that time, they sailed their boats everywhere, and sometimes they didn't go far, and they could catch a lot of fish. Also, because the carp of Green Willow River is very famous, the fish shops quickly took the fish away, and we exchanged the money for things to use. In winter, we stayed in the house to avoid the winter, or went out to find dead trees or something to use as fuel. Sometimes someone angered the gods, the boat capsized, and died, that was also a rare thing. Even there was no such thing.

Later, Green Willow River seemed to be going crazy, rising in water at every turn, and usually roaring like a mad dog. When the big waves came over, we simply had no way to think, praying to the gradually ineffective gods was also useless.

This is nothing. Because our life has trained us to be tough guys, treating life as if it doesn't matter. - Die then die, in twenty years there will be another strong young man. What makes us helpless and only angry is those foreigners' foreign ships. They simply don't have to do anything, just hear the sound of "pulala pulala", and the fish enter their nets. They dress well, eat well, but we suffer: we simply can't live anymore.

Every time I go fishing with my elder brother, we come back disappointed.

Even worse than us are those who are overturned by foreign ships.

My Travel Companion 238

— Yeger

——Miscellaneous Travel Notes Two——

Stepping on the hazy starry night, following the stone-paved path, climbing down step by step, when I looked back up, the seven-treasure pagoda on the top of the temple was already blurred in the dimness. Everyone stopped and casually rested on the rocks by the road. The Jiangxi man, the travel companion I met at the hotel, had already taken off his baggage from his shoulder and sat silently on the stone steps. The small tobacco pouch in his mouth lightly jumped with wisps of sparks, quickly disappearing in the darkness.

A hundred and fifty miles of mountain road is nothing to a porter; but after not being able to find a place to rest last night and rushing all night, he became as desperate as a sick horse, sighing sadly, and then angrily cursing -

"Why?" he roared sadly, "Do we have to run such a cursed mountain road, while people sit securely in the company counting their abacuses, calculating countless profits?..." I ignored him, and after a while he muttered despairingly, as if answering himself, "For, this is life!"

The mountain was quiet, surrounded by darkness. The sharp cries of night birds faintly pierced through from the other side of the forest, quickly echoing and flying away. The Jiangxi man suddenly raised his deep eyes from silence, knocked the ashes from his small tobacco pouch onto the stone steps, hid it on his body, picked up his baggage, stood up, and quietly said, "Let's go!" So we went down the mountain slope step by step again. This time he seemed much more excited, the effect of the small morning tobacco was obvious here. He had forgotten his sighs, and also forgotten his fatigue.

This path is familiar to everyone, especially the Jiangxi man. He told me that twenty years of time had been spent here. "Good buddy," he said, "I can walk this kind of road with my eyes closed, and there won't be any mistakes, but..."

He was deeply troubled by memories. So he began to describe his happy past in a sentimental tone. At that time, he was still young, and had a virtuous and beautiful wife. Not long after they got married, they followed others in the village and went out to rush the mountain road. "At that time, we often didn't feel tired. When everyone felt the threat of hunger, we stopped in the shade of the trees by the road. I took out dry food from my baggage, and she climbed up the ridge like a nimble ape, bringing back a full load of spring water. So we sat on the ground, chewing dry food, and drinking the cold spring water. ... Little buddy, I don't think you'll believe it, she was so beautiful, as beautiful as a happy queen. ...

"We lived such a dreamlike life for three springs. Like a soap bubble, it shattered. All that this world left me was such an emptiness, a terrible lie. ...

"In the year when Chen Lu was advancing to suppress the Tiger Creek Rock bandits, we were just about to return from the inner mountains, and we were intercepted by a team of plainclothes soldiers on the ridge. They said we were spies, stripped us of our clothes, and meticulously checked every pore and corner of our clothes. When I turned to look at my wife, she was also suffering the same humiliation and punishment as me. Her beautiful starry eyes were filled with tears, and her hands deeply covered her face, letting her healthy and full limbs be exposed in the warm sunlight. A crude black man showed a mouthful of yellow teeth, greedily grinning at her, and even stretched out his rough hands to playfully fondle her breasts, causing her whole body to tremble as if electrocuted, and finally she cried out. Friend, you should imagine how much pain was in my heart at that time! I couldn't wait to raise my fist and run over to give these shameless robbers a desperate beating: however, I couldn't, my hands were held by them. So I could only cry out in sorrow, shedding tears.

"Things ended quickly, and we were taken naked to see their officer. The facts proved that we were not bandit spies, and we were released. However, happiness never came to us again. My beautiful wife was worried and sad, and she was shedding tears of hatred so painfully. On the day we were released, without knowing it, her life disappeared on the ridge. She jumped off the top of the mountain and committed suicide. ... Friend, can I not be sad in this kind of life? I have lost happiness, and also lost tenderness. I am such a lonely person, I am old. ..."

The Jiangxi man hoarsely shouted, his throat was choked, and he sobbed and cried.

Nora (14) 239

— Wan Chao Chen, Illustration; Xin Xin, Explanation

Helmer returned, and Nora reiterated her morning request to save Krogstad's position, even if Krogstad's position had been given to Mrs. Linde, she would ask him to dismiss another employee.

Helmer was very angry when he heard this. He said: I don't have weaknesses for people to attack; now the news of Krogstad's dismissal has spread throughout the company. If it spreads outside, it will be said that this new director is being manipulated by his wife - he also explained his difficulties: Krogstad's shortcomings in character may not be worth considering, but Krogstad calling him by his name will damage his dignity. In anger, he called Alan to send out the letter dismissing Krogstad.

Finally, he said, "I'm not afraid of anything. In an emergency, I have the courage to deal with it. My broad shoulders are enough to carry the burden."

He wanted to comfort Nora and returned to his study.

Nora was like a frightened chick.

"Cowardly Hero" Released 247

Locke's Four Years of Hard Work

This year's Paramount Company's valuable production, the famous comedian Locke's latest comedy masterpiece "Cowardly Hero" The Milky Way, has been scheduled to be released in the Great Light Cinema starting today (Wednesday). This handsome and slick king on the screen has not had a new film released for a long time, and the box office success can be predicted. According to him, in his life of filming, except for this "Cowardly Hero," he rarely uses scripts. He is idle all day, thinking about slick materials. In addition, many fans' letters often provide him with jokes. As soon as he has a fresh joke, he immediately takes it down and shoots it into the lens. Therefore, his films always have more jokes than other people's comedies. He is indeed an expert in making jokes. The reason why movie fans all over the world welcome him is because of this reason. In "Cowardly Hero," not only is there an excellent script, but also many excellent jokes made by Locke himself, so it is more brilliant than his previous works. If people in Shanghai need to relieve boredom and laugh heartily, this is a best opportunity not to be missed, and the result will definitely be able to satisfy you.

Silver Miscellany 248

— Editor

Recently, someone has advised me to be careful that movie news is "resting" for no reason, and someone from ×× Film Company called the advertising department of this newspaper (this is Mr. Gao Tianqi of Tianyi Company's old trick, which is not worth a penny when exposed, and it is still anonymous!) I am grateful that they have paid attention to me, this "news editor."

The day before yesterday, I met a friend surnamed Lin, and when we gradually talked about movie news, we talked about the above "problem." It is said that the reason was caused by "Silver Miscellany." Then, since I am the "editor" of "news," it seems necessary to say a few words.

I think the readers of this newspaper can probably prove it for me. The initial Silver Miscellany only "mixed" some news reports and the like, but it also occasionally harmed the bad phenomena in the film industry. So the miscellany caused trouble. It seems like, why don't you do a "news editor" steadily, and insist on "speaking up"? The situation at that time was concealing the readers, punching cold fists in the "darkness" and wanting to "prohibit" people from "speaking up" seemed a bit too "overbearing."

One day, I met Hei Ying at Xinya, and he told me that the thing written under the pen name "Fa Yang" was not written by him; a friend surnamed Lin also told me that "Philosopher" is sometimes not necessarily Mu Shiying's pen name. Then, this situation is very easy to understand, and I don't want to say anything more.

Regarding "Spring Flower," my colleague Mr. Huang received a call from a certain director, who wanted me to do some "things," and I did not do "anything." Maybe that anonymous call came from this, which made me unable to say anything.

In short, this year is not a "peaceful world." I remember that Shi Dongshan wanted to add two dog barks to "Song of Everlasting Regret," which was really right!
